Flour and Wheat Prices Continue to Rise. The Authorities Seek Stabilization Measures. Due to a Lack of Raw Materials, Factories Reduce Production One After Another. Sales of Flour and Wheat from Tianjin and Xi'an Increase Sharply. 100

Da Gong News Agency reports that since flour and wheat prices suddenly rose last Thursday, due to the surge in sales of flour from the Beiyang Gang and manipulation by speculators, market prices have continued to rise, and the price increase has not shown any signs of slowing down. Yesterday was a holiday, but the closing price last Friday was 4.065 yuan for flour expiring this month and 4.1575 yuan for flour expiring in April. The price of wheat expiring this month was 6.54 yuan, the price for wheat expiring in the future was 6.98 yuan, and the price of wheat from Zhongguan had opened at 6.65 yuan. The Tianjin Gang is purchasing nearly 100,000 bags of spot flour, and the number of spot wheat purchased from Xi'an is also very large. Judging from the current situation, it will be difficult to return to a low price when the market opens today.

Striving to Remedy and Stabilize Market Prices

Since the unprecedented surge in flour and wheat prices, the exchange authorities, in order to seek remedies to stabilize market prices, specially solicited opinions from all parties through the board of directors and formulated four measures, announced to both buyers and sellers, and organized an appraisal committee to identify various commodities. The association is scheduled to be established at 2 pm today. The Shanghai Social Affairs Bureau, since the exchange and the brokers' association requested the cancellation of the price limit, and the recent rise in prices is related to the people's livelihood, is now sending staff to the market to conduct investigations to understand the actual situation before handling it.

Flour Mills Reduce Production One After Another

According to Rong Zongjing, a major figure in the flour industry, speaking to a Da Gong News Agency reporter, although there was a good harvest in various parts of the country this year, it is estimated that the Japanese have purchased more than 300,000 dan of domestic wheat. Therefore, the market price has risen accordingly. Farmers and banks that have pledged wheat have hoarded a large amount, resulting in a shortage of spot wheat on the market. Although factories have set up stalls to collect wheat, the number is small. Therefore, manufacturers have reduced the number of vehicles one after another due to insufficient raw materials for flour production. In Shanghai, the number of vehicles in operation is less than 50%. Foreign wheat prices are high and cannot be ordered. The number of flour in factories' warehouses and pledged as collateral is also very limited.

A Large Number of Wheat Boats are Detained Midway

When the Jiwang Temple Police Station of the Jiading County Public Security Bureau detained rice boats in the Wusong River, there were initially eight or nine wheat boats, each with four or five tons, that were also detained. In the past few days, the number of boats passing through has accumulated to more than 20 vessels, and they have not yet been released. Moreover, the wheat was purchased by Shanghai's Shenxin, Fuxin, Xinda, and other factories in the interior. Now that it has been detained, the raw materials for the factories have been interrupted again.

The Tenants Association Sent a Letter to the Real Estate Association, Urging Landlords to Voluntarily Reduce Rents to Lighten Tenants' Burdens and Seek Coexistence and Co-prosperity 103

The Tenants Association of this city believes that although the issue of rent reduction in this city has been repeatedly called for by all parties, requesting the authorities to specify standards, it has not been realized for various reasons. As the end of the year is approaching, various industries are facing even more difficulties. In order to stabilize society, the association sent a letter to the Real Estate Association of this city yesterday, informing the owners to quickly announce a voluntary rent reduction. The original letter stated: "To whom it may concern, the issue of rent reduction in this city has been called for for a long time and has been deadlocked for two years, but the landlords are sticking to their prejudices and have not yet resolved it. In order to achieve the goal of coexistence and co-prosperity, our association has decided through a general meeting to persuade landlords to voluntarily reduce rents by 40% in order to achieve social recovery. We believe that since the January 28th Incident, the commercial situation in Shanghai has become increasingly depressed, and there are daily reports of forced business closures. The reason is that the burden of rent accounts for 50-60% of other expenses. Therefore, the so-called prosperous Shanghai of the past is now filled with empty houses and no one inquires about them. However, the landlords still collect rent from the second landlords on a monthly basis. If they are unable to pay, they resort to legal action. It is important to know that in order for the second landlords to not default on rent, the rent must first be reduced. Then, subletting will be easy and the burden will be lighter, and there will be no more worries about default. Our association has observed this situation, and for the sake of both parties' interests, we hereby request your association to quickly advise the landlords in various places to consider the actual situation and uniformly reduce rents to maintain mutual feelings and make plans for coexistence and co-prosperity. If it is not necessary, we will definitely ask for your understanding. This matter concerns the entire society, and we hope you will adopt it. We are extremely hopeful."

The Fifth Phase of Shanghai County Tobacco Licenses Has Ended 104

A total of 423 licenses re-issued Shanghai County's fifth phase of tobacco user licenses began to be reissued on October, and a method of phased reduction of fees was stipulated. It expired at the end of last month. It is now found that among the tobacco users who exchanged licenses within each time limit, 232 licenses were exchanged in the first time limit, 56 in the second, 21 in the third, 11 in the fourth, and 3 in the fifth, for a total of 323. During the license exchange period, 64 people quit smoking, and 20 people were found to have moved or died due to illness, etc. It is estimated that more than 80% have been reached. Yesterday, County Magistrate Li prepared a document to report the completion situation to the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Civil Affairs for record. On the other hand, the head of the Anti-Smoking Section, Shen Jiaqi, prepared a statistical table and submitted the license fees separately.

Xu Wancheng's Situation is Pitiful 105

His wife died of illness and his bookstore was sealed. Xu Wancheng, a native of Jinshan and the owner of the Longwen Bookstore at the entrance of Baiyang Third Lane, Zhonghua Road, Dananmen, was once detained by the court for more than two months due to the publication of "Xu Wancheng's Work Report Special Issue," which contained an article titled "Investigation of the Dark Secrets of the Chinese Judiciary," which slandered the former President of the Local Court, Luo Tong, and Judge Zhao, etc., for accepting bribes. Later, the High Court transferred jurisdiction to the Wuxian Local Court, which sentenced him to a fine of 30 yuan and announced a reprieve. After the Xu lawsuit was resolved, he filed an appeal on the one hand, and on the other hand, he also accused Luo Tong and Judge Fu Hongze and Prosecutor Tang Ruxiu, etc., of improper detention, which was also handed over to the Wuxian Local Court by the High Court for trial. Just as he was about to show his talent, bad luck came one after another. His wife recently died of illness. Moreover, the house where Xu Wancheng rented and opened the Longwen Bookstore was sued by the landlord Luo Yaqing for owing 480 yuan in rent during the period when Xu Wancheng was involved in the lawsuit. After the judgment was confirmed, the Local Court ordered the bailiffs to go to the Longwen Bookstore to execute all the business assets and seal the store on the previous day. Xu Wancheng's situation can truly be described as family ruin and death.

A Kidnapping Case Was Cracked at the Osaka Wharf, and Three Children Were Rescued 106

The five-year-old boys Gengen and Linlin, sons of Yao Jin Shi and Yao Bu Shi, women from Pudong at No. 14 Yanhai Road, Huajie, and the six-year-old boy Jusheng, son of Cai Xing, a native of Ningbo at No. 3 Fangbang Road, went missing while playing at the door between the 20th and 25th of last month. The Public Security Bureau reported the case and arrested the kidnappers. There were no clues to be found. Until about 2 p.m. on the 26th, Feng Shaoshan, a Chinese detective from the Huishan Police Station, discovered two Ningbo women, Wang Li Shi and Chen Ye Shi, on the Japanese ship Shengjing Maru at the Osaka Wharf in Yangshupu. They were planning to send the three children to Fujian to sell them for profit. They were brought to the police station together. Later, a fellow gang member, Zhu Shunchang from Zhenjiang, was found at Wang Li Shi's house at No. 5, Lane 70, Caishi Road, in the French Concession. He was also escorted to the First Special District Court for detention and sent to the Public Security Bureau for transfer. All three children were taken back by their families. Yesterday, Judge Xiao Xie Fen questioned the three defendants in the third criminal court, and since the Public Security Bureau still did not send Chang to court, it was decided to transfer the three defendants to the Shanghai Local Court for review.

The Lawyers Association Collects Clothes and Bedding for Prisoners. The Weather is Severe and Prisoners are Crying Out. Kind People Should Donate. 107

The Shanghai Lawyers Association believes that the number of detainees in the Jiangsu High Court Detention Center, the Shanghai Second Special District Local Court Prison, and the Jiangsu Second Prison is large. Recently, due to the severe weather, they cry out and weep at night because they lack prisoners' clothes and bedding. The prison wardens of these prisons sent letters to the association a few days ago, requesting donations of clothes and bedding so that each prisoner could keep warm, etc. The association submitted it to the Executive Committee for discussion and decided to notify all its members to enthusiastically donate clothes and bedding within two weeks, which would be collected and transferred to the prisons for distribution to the prisoners to keep warm, etc. The association notified all members yesterday to generously donate clothes and bedding and send them to the association for transfer within two weeks. Then, public morality will be immeasurable.

Hong Yuanyuan is Unfaithful, Her Husband Catches Her in the Act 108

Huang Yongkang, a native of Changshu, 18 years old, an optician, and resident of No. 407 Zhaojiabang Road, married Hong Yuanyuan (19 years old), a local woman, in January of last year. After the marriage, they were still harmonious. Before long, it became clear that she was involved in extramarital affairs, and her husband could not keep an eye on her because of his business. Recently, he heard that she was having an affair with Lin Hongjie (29 years old), a local man who worked in a rice shop. Huang entrusted his friend Feng Yonghai to tail her. Sure enough, the previous night, he saw Lin Hongjie and Hong attending a movie at the Zhejiang Grand Theater. They followed them to the Central Hotel in Xiaodongmen, and then reported to Huang Yongkang to catch them in the act. They were caught naked and brought to the Yimiao Police Station by the police for investigation. After interrogation, it was found that the case involved adultery, and they were ordered to be sent to the General Bureau for review.

The Weather in This Port is Severe 109

Since a brief snow flurry the night before last, the weather in this port was even more severe yesterday morning. The north wind was blowing frequently, and it was extremely cold. Water storage appliances were frozen into thin layers, as were ditches. Moreover, the sunlight was sometimes visible and sometimes hidden, and the weather was uncertain. The French and Chinese Water Company, in view of the fact that the weather has entered the deep winter, reminded residents to pay attention to the anti-freeze measures for their water taps and meters. Dry grass should be used to wrap them to prevent them from freezing and cracking or being blocked by ice.

The Ice River is Near Dagu Port and the Navigation Marks have been Removed 110

Lightships and light buoys replaced by black posts. The Customs Service has decided to remove all navigation marks at Dagu Port after December 1 due to the arrival of winter and the proximity of the ice river at Dagu Port. Except for the deep waterway light buoys, all other buoys and light lanes will be replaced by black cylindrical mooring posts in their original locations. However, the deep waterway light buoys will be replaced by a wooden marker with a suspended spherical mark on the side of the abandoned river dike. The names of the above-mentioned original lightships, buoys, etc. are listed below: (1) Dagu Lightship, (2) Dagu Import Light Buoy, (3) Dagu Sand Tail Buoy, (4) Waterway Test Guide Buoy, (5) Deep Waterway Light Buoy, (6) Gulanjiang Sand Lightship,

Group Wedding, 12th Session Begins Registration 111

The group wedding organized by the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau has reached its eleventh session and achieved remarkable results. It has now been decided that registration for the twelfth wedding will begin today and end on the 21st of this month. The wedding ceremony is scheduled to be held in the Municipal Government Auditorium on February 3 next year. Citizens who wish to participate can directly write to the Public Welfare Section of the Fourth Department of the Bureau to request an application form and follow the regulations. As for the previous rumors that the Bureau's future group weddings will be held in the Municipal Stadium, it is said that this is a misunderstanding.

The Li Guojie Case - The Execution Court Opens Today. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Requests Strict Enforcement. The Court Will Summon Two Guarantors for Questioning. 112

Li Guojie, the former general manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, mortgaged the four wharves to the China Business Company during his tenure and embezzled more than 700,000 taels of public funds and bribed Chen Fumu, the former director of the company. After three trials, Li was sentenced to eight months of imprisonment with a suspended sentence. The principal and interest of his private lawsuit have reached more than 1.2 million yuan. During the execution hearing, Li Guojie was released on bail by Chu Qiqing and Li Sihao, but they have not yet paid. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has also offered a reward to find Li's property, but only a small portion, less than one-tenth, has been found. They have repeatedly urged the lawsuit and requested that Li Guojie be declared bankrupt by official authority. Li's side stated that he has a considerable position in society and expressed his unwillingness to be executed. Judge Yu Lude ordered Li to provide property within half a month, but at the deadline, Li requested an extension due to illness. The plaintiff's attorney requested strict enforcement in court. The judge ruled that he would summon the guarantors for questioning and then review the matter. The execution court of the Local Court has scheduled a hearing today to question the matter.

National Defense Art Society Holds Third Preparatory Meeting 113

Holding an Air Defense Painting Exhibition

Organizing National Defense Song Broadcasts

The Guomin News Agency reports that the National Defense Art Society, after more than a month of preparation, is now beginning to take shape. The society held its third preparatory meeting yesterday, deciding on the work to be carried out during the preparatory period. Those present included Chuan Bolang, Zhang Meisun, Tan Chuantuan, Kang Zhuying, Liang Wanli, Song Qiqin, Shi Wenbin, Yan Keding, etc., who unanimously elected Yan Keding as chairman and Chuan Bolang as secretary. First, it was reported that the number of participating members had reached one hundred, with members from Anhui, Hankou, Hangzhou, Suzhou, Nanchang, Wuxi, Changshu, and other places participating. The following resolutions were discussed: (1) In order to encourage more enthusiastic participation from artists throughout the city, the establishment was postponed. (2) To expand the recruitment of members, Yan Keding was nominated to draft a letter to artists throughout the city. (3) To first establish a temporary editorial committee to actively compile national defense paintings, music, and craft teaching materials, and Zhang Meisun, Shi Chongpeng, Chuan Bolang, and nineteen others were nominated as members. (4) It was decided to stage a drama performance early next year, organize a performance committee, and Yan Keding, He Kangli, and five others were nominated as members, with Wu Keding concurrently serving as general affairs and He Kangli as stage manager. The script has been decided as "Our Homeland I," directed by the author Zhang Min et al. (5) To hold an exhibition and meeting on air defense, poison gas defense, and bandit suppression paintings, and Liang Xiaohong, Xiong Zuolin, and eleven others were nominated as preparatory members. (6) To prepare a special radio station to broadcast national defense songs, and Kang Zhuying and eleven others were nominated as preparatory members, and after contact with the city's Mutual Aid Society, it was initially decided that the broadcast material would be "Anti-Enemy Song," etc. Mr. Chuan Bolang of the society has compiled a method for manufacturing gas masks, which can be obtained by sending a letter with ten cents in postage to the address (published by the Zhonghua Art Company on Penglai Road). Kang Zhuying and others have already begun compiling multiple volumes of national defense song collections, which will be published soon. Now, we will explore and adopt the society's enlarged solicitation of members, as stated in its letter to art educators in the city, as follows:

Since the National Defense Art Society was permitted to organize by Party and government organs, it has been actively preparing with the support of all parties, and the society's affairs are progressing daily. Many art teachers in the city have participated enthusiastically, but there are still many who have not. Considering the reason, it is because the purpose and objectives of the society have not been understood by all. Therefore, we will restate several points as follows: First, to enhance national awareness. Art is the expression of human life, and the nation is the sum of human collective life. At this time of imminent danger for China, the collective life of the Chinese nation may be destroyed. If we want to ensure the continuation and development of this collective life, we should actively utilize the effectiveness of art to enhance national awareness. This is the first point. Second, to promote national spirit. Art is the expression of the human spirit, and the nation is the highest form of human life. Chinese people's lives have always been decadent, scattered, narrow, disorganized. If we want to make the Chinese nation develop upward, we must actively utilize the effectiveness of art to promote the national spirit. This is the second point. Third, to build national strength. Art has the creation of human strength, and the nation is the result of the creation of human strength. Due to internal geographic relations, the lives of Chinese people have always been conservative and biased towards regional concepts, unable to create a collective national strength. If we want to resist national demise and make the Chinese nation forever prosperous and sustainable, we must actively utilize the effectiveness of art to build national strength. This is the third point. The above three points are the greatest purposes and objectives of the society's organization. We hope that art educators in the city will not hesitate to offer corrections and look forward to their enthusiastic participation to discuss and carry out these three tasks. All comrades, why not come?

New Drug Industry Requests Purchase of Sealed Narcotics 117

The National Federation of New Drug Associations submitted a request to the Ministry of Health yesterday, stating that the request is to purchase the narcotic drugs sealed nationwide at a price to alleviate the difficulties of merchants. It is hoped that it will be reviewed and approved. It is humbly believed that the "Provisional Measures for Purchasing and Using Narcotic Drugs" stipulates that morphine and up to ten other types can be purchased and used. However, there are no clear regulations on how to deal with the other types. However, before the promulgation of these measures, member businesses still had unsold inventory of the other ten types. If they continue to be used, it would violate the law. If they are simply destroyed, significant capital would be at stake. Since the law does not apply retroactively, this type of inventory was purchased legally before the promulgation of the regulations for legitimate use. If it is not properly disposed of, it seems unfair in terms of both sentiment and reason. Therefore, the member association submitted a request to your department, requesting permission to sell out the inventory to provide relief. It was humbly approved on January 29th, Medical Document No. 426, stating that the request has been noted, and the merchants should be notified to quickly list the types and quantities of their inventory and report them for further review. This approval was followed by Medical Document No. 3974 on July 16th, stating that the request has been noted and continued inquiries should be made to expedite the reporting. Because of this, the member association has repeatedly urged all member businesses to quickly report and has repeatedly reported to your department for record. However, there have been no instructions on how to handle this inventory. Now, the second National Congress of Member Representatives has raised the issue for discussion. All agreed that the inventory is a matter of significant capital, and prolonged sealing will have a negative impact. Therefore, it was resolved to appeal to your department to observe the difficulties of the people and approve the purchase of the narcotic drugs sealed nationwide at a price to alleviate the difficulties of merchants, which would be a great kindness.

Jiang Yao Xianhui Lectures on Married Life Yesterday 122

Three Points to Note in Married Life, Mutual Understanding Can Reduce Misunderstandings

Ms. Jiang Yao Xianhui, former director of the Student Department of the Young Women's Christian Association, gave a detailed lecture on "Married Life and Spiritual Cultivation" at the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA at 4 PM yesterday. Ms. Jiang said that in the past, Chinese women's married life emphasized self-cultivation, such as the "Three Obediences and Four Virtues" of the old etiquette. Therefore, women in large families only had obedience and patience. Today, with the progress of the times and the influence of European and American freedom, young men and women have abandoned large family life and organized small families, and advocate spousal autonomy. With reasonable marriage freedom, small family life is bound to be harmonious. However, married life cannot be entirely satisfactory. We can make up for this shortcoming only by paying attention to spiritual cultivation. However, this kind of cultivation should be different from the passive obedience and "patience" of the past, and pay attention to (1) mutual understanding, (2) appreciative attitude, (3) playful attitude. Because mutual understanding can reduce misunderstandings, paying attention to an appreciative attitude can enable both parties to understand each other's strengths, and a playful life can dissolve serious family problems and achieve harmony.

Tram Collides with Bus on Xinzha Road 127

Tram Smashes Bus Window, Bus Remains Unscathed

At around 4:15 PM yesterday, at the intersection of Xinzha Road and Xinzha Bridge in the International Settlement, a No. 15015 Route 10 bus was driving eastward when a No. 32 locomotive pulling a No. 255 trailer from Magan Road to Dongxin Bridge approached from behind. Because the road was narrow, the Route 10 bus was close to the tram tracks, causing the trailer of the tram to collide with the bus. There was a loud crash, and the bus window shattered immediately. Fortunately, there were not many passengers, and they knew to avoid the impact, so no one was injured. Chinese and Western police officers arrived, recorded the numbers of both drivers, and briefly halted traffic. Traffic then resumed.

Boatman Attempts to Sell Stolen Gasoline 128

Scheme Unsuccessful, Arrested

Liu San, 44 years old from Taizhou, used to work as a boatman. Recently, he learned that Wuxi Huacheng Company and Yixing Yushun Company purchased eighty barrels of gasoline each from Texaco in this city, totaling 9,600 yuan at 60 yuan per barrel. They entrusted Xue Youji Transportation Company at Xinmatou, Nanshi, to transport it. Liu had a sudden idea and colluded with unemployed boatmen Wang Zhenlong, Cai Douyou, and Ming Fu to steal a No. 8272 pier boat belonging to an unknown boatman. Liu pretended to be the boat owner and solicited the business from Mei Jinhua, a broker at Xue Youji, to transport the gasoline to Guanxi. The freight he quoted was very low. Mei did not know Liu and dared not trust him. Liu then incited Pu Jinbao and Bing Xiaonan to act as guarantors, and they finally agreed on a deal. On the 2nd of this month, Liu loaded 160 barrels of gasoline onto the boat and left Shanghai. Liu believed his opportunity had arrived, and Yan Juhong facilitated the sale of the large quantity of gasoline to Liu and Shen Quansheng, who specialized in small goods. Just as they were negotiating the price, Xue Youji became anxious because the goods had not arrived at their destination. Jiang Gensheng, a broker at Zhengtai Transportation Company, learned of the matter and confronted Liu in Shanghai. Liu did not reveal anything, but Jiang quietly learned of their whereabouts and quickly reported to Mei Jinhua, requesting the customs water police to investigate. After receiving the report, the police sent detectives Hu Changqing and Jin Guifu to arrest Liu, who confessed to fraudulently transporting the gasoline with the intention of selling it. The stolen goods had not yet been unloaded, and the boat was moored near Qiwu Road, Yangshupu. The detectives then recovered all the stolen goods and summoned the original guarantors Pu and Bing for questioning. Based on Liu's confession, they also went to Room 22 of the Sanjiang Inn on North Hai Road at 5:30 AM yesterday and arrested another accomplice, Cai Douyou. They were detained to continue the arrest of the remaining fugitives and handle the case.

Threw Filth, Sentenced to 50 Days of Detention 129

Jin Zhiqing (40 years old, from Changshu), an employee of the Shanghai Chinese Cloth Exchange on Avenue Edward VII, left the exchange at noon on the 1st of this month and took a chartered car back to his residence at No. 10 Rue des Soeurs when, while the car was passing by the Central Bank of China, a rogue named Tu Jinlang from Jiangxi suddenly rushed out from the side of the road, stopped Jin's chartered car, and threw the dung contained in a paper bag in his hand onto Jin's head and face, causing Jin's mouth and nose to be covered in dirt, and his clothes and hat to be dripping with filth and unbearable stench. Jin got out of the car and chased after him, shouting loudly, and was caught by the police, who took him to the police station and sent him to the Second Special Court for interrogation and detention. The investigation of the circumstances has been recorded in this newspaper. The presiding judge, Zhang Minsheng, conducted a preliminary hearing in the Eighth Criminal Division the previous morning. The police attorney Chen Ming and the police station investigated the case and filed a lawsuit in accordance with the law. Then, the plaintiff testified about the situation of being dirtied. The defendant confessed that the plaintiff's chartered car had torn his clothes, and he had asked for compensation but was refused, so he held a grudge and threw the dung. The court verified the confession and sentenced Tu Jinlang to fifty days of detention for damaging the property of others, as a warning.

Fresh Pork Vendors Association's Letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce 135

The Fresh Pork Vendors Association sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, stating: "Respectfully informing you that we have received a joint letter from 34 vendors, including Xu Zhongliu of Nantong County, Sang Lixuan, Qin Guojun and Cong Yixing of Rugao County, Zhang Yiyuan and Sha Wenxuan of Dongtai County, etc., stating that the Jiangbei pork business tax violates provincial orders by arbitrarily establishing tax checkpoints, abusing power, and harming the people. We urge you to forward this to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, who will then forward it to the Executive Yuan, to retrieve and review the full files of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance and the detailed original documents from the Nantong Administrative Inspector Commissioner, to gather witnesses from both sides, and to investigate and punish fairly according to the law. Furthermore, reserve the right to recover losses and damages to deter corruption and maintain provincial governance. The establishment of the Jiangbei pork business tax is based on the practice of Anhui Province, where the industry association collects taxes on behalf of the government. Collection points are set up at various river ports, as these are where pork businesses congregate, thus the regulation of industry association collection avoids taxing goods directly, preventing conflict with the gold tax abolition case. It also prevents tax collectors from harassing merchants and causing undue difficulties. However, the business tax commissioner Chen Gao and the contractors Bao Shang and Tang, have set up nine checkpoints in the Dingyan, Baipu, Liqiao, Maqiao, and Matang areas at the Tong-Rugao border, intercepting ships along the river to collect taxes on pork. Some of these, such as the five Yu checkpoints, were not even established during the Likin era, or were set up during the Likin surplus era but were later abolished by order of the provincial government after being reported as illegal. The business tax bureau has recently re-established them all, ignoring repeated complaints. Here are the specific violations and harms caused by the unauthorized establishment of five checkpoints to intercept ships for tax collection: (1) It violates the original plan to abolish Likin and add taxes, taxing goods. (2) It violates the original provincial order that industry associations collect taxes on behalf of the government, setting up checkpoints in inland river areas where there are no industry associations. (3) It re-establishes checkpoints at places that were already ordered to be abolished, such as the Liao Yan and Matang, and sets up new checkpoints without approval, such as Liqiao and Maqiao, defying laws, harming the country, and harming the people. (4) Within the same tax collection area, Jingjiang, Rugao, and Nantong have different methods and vastly different tax rates, disrupting the business of our Nantong people, merchants, rickshaw pullers, and boatmen, making it impossible to maintain a livelihood. (5) Because they have privately added five checkpoints to intercept taxes mid-river, merchants from Dongtai and Rugao exporting pork from Nantong are subjected to economic pressure, have difficulty in turnover, business shrinks, time is extended, prices are devalued and sold cheaply, and there are various losses such as death and damage. The first three items are violations of national law and defiance of provincial orders by the business tax bureau, while the latter two items are the destruction of the business of merchants and the livelihoods of farmers, rickshaw pullers, and boatmen. Based on these facts, the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, along with transport merchants Yin Hegao and Zhang Yiyuan, have appealed one after another, but the tax bureau, relying on backing, has delayed until now and refuses to abolish the checkpoints. Recently, they have become even more unscrupulous in exploiting the people. Zhongliu and others have petitioned the Nantong Administrative Inspector Commissioner's Office, requesting a thorough investigation and relief according to the law. It has also been verified that the business tax bureau collects taxes on behalf of the industry association at Xingang and other places, assesses the value of goods at Xinshenggang and other places, and sets up checkpoints on ships in the middle of inland rivers in Nantong to assess and collect taxes, which is actually a method of collecting taxes on individual pigs (with attached documents). The methods of collection are inconsistent, which is indeed the case. As for the disparity in tax rates and other malpractices, they have not yet been investigated, but even just the point of setting up checkpoints in inland rivers and inconsistent collection methods is enough to show that there is indeed harassment of merchants. Furthermore, according to the Ministry of Finance's document No. 4752, the provincial government has already prohibited the establishment of checkpoints in inland rivers. Therefore, the business tax bureau should follow the original plan and unify the collection methods to avoid criticism. From a legal standpoint, this case should be forwarded to the provincial government for review. All of these cases show that the bureau's lawlessness and harm to the people are as clear as day. However, several months have passed, and the bureau has not yet abolished the checkpoints in inland rivers, nor has it followed the original plan of collection by industry associations as stipulated by the provincial government, despite repeated orders from the provincial government. It seems that the pork business tax bureau, as a legally established national institution, should be based on national laws and be subject to the command of the provincial government, rather than being allowed to defy laws and orders and trample on the people. Its arrogance and audacity to abuse power and harm the people, and the appeals and official documents that fill the desks, have not been straightened out, leaving us common people with no law to rely on and at their mercy. Now, we are preparing the reasons, attaching supporting documents and diagrams, and sending this letter to your association, according to the original letter, to forward it to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, who will then forward it to the Executive Yuan for review. We hope that you will consider the plight of the merchants, provide prompt relief, and in the spirit of filial piety, unleash the power of thunder, and immediately order the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance to retrieve and review all relevant documents regarding the establishment of the business tax bureau, the full file of the people's organization's complaints against the bureau's violations, and the detailed original request from the Nantong Administrative Inspector Commissioner, and to gather witnesses from both sides for questioning as soon as possible to alleviate their suffering. As for the damages suffered by various industries in Tongfang due to the bureau's violations, please order them to be reserved and separately pursued for compensation, and report them together. This would be a great act of kindness, and we are extremely grateful." It is permissible to investigate the truth. Check the attached map of the exit from the river, and there are as many as 20 locations. It is true that corvée is frightening to hear. The rescue team has repeatedly requested assistance from the meeting. The meeting sent a letter to the council to call for assistance, but the local government of Jiangsu Province did not thoroughly investigate and punish the spirit of party rule. Since the abolition of the levy card for several years, the merchants' suffering has not been relieved. Back to the people, the national abolition of the levy card was completed in the year of the revolution. Since then, the province has been closely linked to the capital, and it is a strange thing to violate the national laws and decrees. This kind of corruption and abuse of power is a national curse. With the approval of the letter, a copy of the map of the Jiangbei pig's export from the river is attached, and two photos are sent to your society, and a letter is sent to the Executive Yuan to investigate the greed and evils in accordance with the law, and to maintain the imperative urgency.

Central Land Grab Involves Shanghai Islamic Association Calls Emergency Meeting 136

Telegraphs the entire nation to unite in support

The Nanjing Central University plans to build a new campus, selecting over 2,000 acres of mountainous land outside the Zhonghua Gate in Nanjing, including thousands of Islamic graves, to be confiscated on a set date. This has triggered serious negotiations from Islamic individuals across the country. A few days ago, the Nanjing Islamic Cemetery Protection Association sent representatives Mai Guomin and Gai Shaofeng to Shanghai. They gave a brief report at the Fuyou Road Mosque in the city on the previous day (the Islamic congregational prayer day), with an audience of six to seven hundred people. The Shanghai Islamic Association received an official letter from the Nanjing Islamic Cemetery Protection Association and held an emergency meeting at the Fuyou Road Mosque yesterday (6th) at 3 PM. The entire executive committee of the association and representatives from Nanjing attended. Chairman Wu Yongxia presided over the meeting. A decision was made on the spot to telegraph Islamic followers nationwide to unite in support, and to telegraph the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Education, and other agencies, requesting them to understand the Muslims' hardship of not being able to move graves after death and to order Central University to find a new location to accord with public opinion. It is also heard that Islamic individuals in Shanghai plan to petition the municipal government within days and will not stop until their goal is achieved.

Songjiang Fellow-Provincials Association Actively Prepares for Next Month's Establishment 137

Club and Dormitory Open, Consumer Cooperative Ready

Tens of thousands of Songjiang fellow-provincials live in Shanghai, but they lack a perfect organization, leading to indifference to each other's welfare. Now, Wu Kaixian, Ma Yinliang, Zhang Xiaotong, Geng Jiaji, and others from Songjiang living in Shanghai have initiated the establishment of the Songjiang Fellow-Provincials Association to serve fellow-provincials and the local community. It has been filed with the municipal party and government agencies and is actively carrying out preparations. The association's premises have been leased, and they are quite spacious. They are recruiting members, have hired a white team leader, and are proceeding separately. Enrollment is quite enthusiastic. It is heard that it can be formally established next month. It is also known that the association's affiliated members' club and dormitory have been opened ahead of schedule, and the consumer cooperative is also ready. It is further known that the association has a large hall for fellow-provincials to rent for celebrations and gatherings. There are also office spaces for rent, such as for lawyers, accountants, or firms. The affiliated communications office is very welcome. For detailed information, please contact the association's preparatory office at No. 1 Wubenfang, Caishi Road, Fiddes Road, telephone 82798.

Transportation Industry Association Held Fourth Representative Congress The Day Before Yesterday 138

The Transportation Industry Association convened its fourth member representative congress the day before yesterday, with over 130 attendees. Chairman Rang Jimulian, Dong Zihua, and He Bingxiang discussed the proposed motions: (1) Regarding the number of membership fees stipulated in the association's charter, it was proposed to reduce the amount. It was resolved to change it to 150 yuan. (2) Appraisal of convenience fees. It was resolved: (A) Whole car export, 20 cents per ton; (B) Whole car import, 15 cents per ton; (C) LTL import, changed to 5 cents per 100 kg, less than 100 kg will be considered as 100 kg. LTL export, add 10% to the railway bureau's freight rate. (3) Regarding the association's insufficient budget, how to organize it. It was resolved to let the next executive committee find a way to organize it, and to collect membership fees in different grades. It was resolved to temporarily maintain the status quo. (4) Moving the association's premises to save expenses. It was resolved not to move temporarily. (5) For goods transported by the railway, the owner must still be responsible for the sale, and a 10% fee should not be added. It was resolved to hand it over to the next executive committee to find out the types of goods and forward it to the Ministry of Railways for review. (6) The railway's regulations for goods calculated by square feet should be corrected to uniformly add 50% freight. It was resolved to hand it over to the next executive committee to clarify the types of goods that should not be subject to the 50% freight increase and forward it to the Ministry of Railways for revision. (7) Regarding the railway's heavy fines, it was requested to strive for improvement from the Ministry of Railways. It was resolved to petition the Ministry of Railways. (8) Regarding the acquisition of the original association premises at the South Station, it was resolved to retain it. (9) The Shanghai North Station's freight yard is narrow, and goods are often received in the open air. All goods are pre-marked (wetness at one's own risk). It was resolved to hand it over to the next executive committee to forward it to the Railway Bureau for correction. A portion of the executive and supervisory committee members had completed their terms. The congress re-elected Shen Jiefu, Fei Xiangfu, Guo Yehui, Yu Xinchuan, Chen Shiying, Wang Zhaosun, He Shengzhi, and Du Chuncui as executive committee members, and Zhou Renqing, Fang Jiren, and Dong Zihua as supervisory committee members.

Weather Report 145

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: The weather around Shandong is clear and cold, with northwesterly winds. The Yellow River Basin has southwesterly to northwesterly winds. The middle and upper reaches of the Yangtze River are overcast, with a risk of rain and uncertain wind direction. The lower reaches of the Yangtze River are cloudy and stuffy, with fog and northwesterly to northeasterly winds. There is rain in several places in the East China Sea and Taiwan, with regular seasonal winds. The center of the gale moved to within 120 miles of 15 degrees north latitude and 115 degrees east longitude at 6 AM and is gradually dissipating. The wind force is unknown. Furthermore, in the 24 hours before 3 PM yesterday, the local temperature was a maximum of 46.8 and a minimum of 36.1. On the same day last year, the maximum was 64.2 and the minimum was 37.0.

Robbery and Murder Case: Gao Hongbang Not Guilty; Gao Was in Nanjing When the Crime Occurred; The Circuit Court Verified the Facts 146

On the evening of May 27th last year at 9:45 PM, the home of Zhang Juyang, a Siyang native residing at 70 Yangshupu Road, was invaded by several armed bandits, who robbed property worth 549 yuan, fled, and opened fire, fatally wounding their accomplice Chen Buzhao, and wounding Zhang and his friend Shi Jinzhu. After being apprehended by the police, the perpetrators Ma Jinbiao, Wang Jinsheng, Wang Fu, and others were sent to the First Special District Court and sentenced to various prison terms. They confessed that the middleman was a person named "Little Pipe" who was at large and could not be found. On the morning of October 20th of this year, the Chinese and foreign detectives of the Yangshupu Police Station received a tip from an informant that "Little Pipe" was Gao Hongbang from Haizhou, hiding in a bungalow on Haizhou Road. They secretly arrested him and sent him to court for repeated trials, but he did not admit to the crime. However, the settled perpetrators Ma Jinbiao et al. identified him in their proposals, all saying that "Little Pipe" was not the defendant. Gao said that he was in Nanjing at the time, staying with a friend of Li Jihai at Longwang Temple, for a month. For the sake of caution, the court sent a letter to the Capital District Court to verify the facts, which confirmed his alibi. The defendant hired lawyer Fan Gang to defend him. The ruling was heard. Yesterday, Judge Zhong Qing of the Criminal Division 3 ruled Gao Hongbang not guilty and released him.

Overview of Changes in Shanghai Industry and Commerce in September 1936 (Continued) 147

— Edited by China Credit

(Shanghai Industry and Commerce Overview, No. 39)

(6) Li Maochang Machine Copper and Iron Bed Factory Liquidates and Sells: The factory was established around 1918-1919, sixteen or seventeen years ago. The registered capital was seven or eight thousand yuan. It was founded solely by Mr. Li Liancai and employed fifteen or sixteen workers. The total value of machinery and equipment was over three thousand yuan. Since its opening, the initial scope was small. After Mr. Li's painstaking management, the foundation gradually stabilized. The sales of its products were mainly to hotels in the Beijing area. In recent years, it has been affected by the economic downturn externally and competition from peers internally, resulting in a decline in business, difficult turnover, and heavy losses, forcing it to liquidate and sell.

(7) China Lead Wire Manufacturing Co., Ltd. Established: The company was initiated by Mr. Chen Jingtang and Mr. Zhang Songshan. The annual demand for lead wire in China is huge, but no one in the country has set up a factory to manufacture it, relying on imports from abroad every year. Therefore, Mr. Chen and others, in order to promote production and prevent leakage, joined forces with like-minded people to establish China Lead Wire Manufacturing Co., Ltd. to manufacture in Shanghai. All shares have been subscribed by the founders separately, and a shareholders' meeting was formally established on the 10th of this month, electing Jiang Yiping, Chen Jingtang, Fang Yixian, Zhang Songshan, Zhu Rushan, Dai Gengxin, and Zhang Liling as directors, and Shao Jingfu and Xiang Meiying as supervisors.

In the sales and commercial category this month, the number of new businesses increased slightly compared to last month, while the number of closures increased by twenty compared to last month, and the situation seems to have deteriorated again. The main reason for this is the decline of the cotton cloth, Western clothing, and department store industries. The more important changes are as follows:

(1) Hongchang Cloth Shop Temporarily Ceases Business: The shop was founded in 1932 and has been in operation for over four years. The manager is Mr. Zheng Xiaozhong. Business has been fairly successful on weekdays, and there have been surpluses in recent years. Recently, due to differences of opinion among shareholders, there have been many twists and turns. The disputes between the manager and shareholders are serious, making it impossible to continue the business, forcing it to temporarily cease operations. The outside world is very sorry for this.

(2) Weida Silk and Satin Store Opens: The store was initiated by silk industry magnates Liu Mingjia, Yu Zhongfei, and Shen Disheng and started preparations in the spring of this year. They leased the shop base at the intersection of Nanjing Road and Guangxi Road and rebuilt the facade themselves. The work was completed last month. After active arrangements, it opened on the 20th of this month. Internally, it is divided into silk and satin, new clothing, trims, suiting materials, wholesale, mail order, and gift certificate departments. The scale is grand and the equipment is novel, making it a rising star in the silk industry.

(3) Tongkangxiang Foreign Goods and Cotton Cloth Shop Temporarily Ceases Business: The shop has been open for many years and has a large scope. It is organized as a partnership, with shareholder Mr. Xu Fengyi concurrently serving as manager. The capital is strong, and it has a reputation in the industry. Business has also been fairly successful on weekdays. Unexpectedly, there was a sudden internal organizational relationship recently, forcing it to cease business and liquidate. The responsible persons left separately, causing great panic among the creditors. It is heard that a creditors' group has been organized to negotiate.

(4) Zhendachang Yarn and Thread Shop Opens: The shop was founded jointly by yarn industry figures Gu Xikun, Shao Huikang, Wu Mulian, and others. The scale is grand, and the capital is strong. It specializes in Chinese and foreign cotton yarn, various coarse and fine threads, cotton silk, wool, cashmere, etc., as well as various raw materials for cotton mills and knitting factories, and refined mercerized dyeing. It opened on the 3rd of this month.

(5) Yuanfengrun Incense and Candle Shop Closes: The shop was founded solely by Mr. Zhang Geyuan and is a giant in the candle industry. Its high reputation and long history are well known to people in Shanghai. It is heard that it has been open for over twenty years, and with proper management, there have been annual surpluses. Branch stores have been set up in Hangzhou and Putuo, further strengthening its position. Outside deposits have been increasing steadily. Mr. Zhang used the surplus funds to set up the Tiandetang Pharmacy and an inland shipping company, but both failed, resulting in heavy losses. Mr. Zhang was greatly weakened by this blow. Although the candle shop still has a surplus, it is a drop in the bucket. The debt is accumulating, and the economic turnover is difficult. The creditors have filed lawsuits in court one after another, and the court has executed a seizure. Although Mr. Zhang tried his best to communicate with the creditors and suggested transferring the debt into shares in order to revive the business, it was ultimately impossible to recover due to the creditors' tough attitude. As a result, this once-renowned candle shop painfully closed down.

(6) Zhonghua National Goods Company Opens: The company was founded by industrialists Zhou Beilin and Zhou Jingkang, with a registered capital of 200,000 yuan in national currency. Internally, it is divided into silk and satin, leather shoes, knitwear, cotton textiles, and hat departments. Some spaces are rented to other operators. The scale is quite large, and it is a strong force in the national goods industry.

(7) Beifu Foreign Goods Store Opens: The store is a large-scale shopping mall established by Japanese merchants, specializing in silk, cotton, and wool fabrics, cosmetics, toys, stationery, and other items. It opened on the 2nd of this month. It is said that the company plans to set up branches in Hongkou and other important areas in due course.

(8) Cheap Shopping Mall Closes: The shopping mall only opened on March 10th of this year and has suddenly announced a temporary cessation of business after only half a year. It is heard that the shopping mall was originally founded by a coalition of national goods manufacturers, and its nature was not a permanent organization. (To be continued)

1937 Davis Cup Schedule Announcement by the British Lawn Tennis Association 150

Since the board of directors of the National Sports Advancement Association resolved to participate in next year’s (1937) Davis Cup World Tennis Tournament, it has officially telegraphed its registration. It is now learned that the association received a letter from the British Lawn Tennis Association, the host country of the Davis Cup World Tennis Tournament, notifying the schedule for the European Zone competition and the dates for the Challenge Round, etc., as follows:

European Zone

First week: May 4th, end

Second week: May 16th, end

Third week: June 8th, end

Fourth week: June 17th, end

Final: July 12th

Inter-Zone Final: July 17th, 19th, 23rd

Challenge Round: July 24th, 26th, 27th, 3rd

Registration for the European Zone closes on January 30, 1937.

The representatives' meeting of various countries is scheduled to be held in London on July 26, 1937.

With Feng Scoring Two Penalty Kicks, Tung Wah Fortunately Defeats Western Police; Western Police Once Led 4-2 and Was Celebrated for a Time; Unfortunately, Two Own Goals and Two Penalty Kicks Reversed the Situation, Allowing Tung Wah to Achieve a Final Victory of 6-4. 151

Tung Wah and Western Police met yesterday in the second week of the Scotto Cup competition at the Recreation Ground. The scene was quite crowded. Tung Wah played cautiously, and Western Police showed no weakness either. In the first half, they even took a 3-2 lead, making the entire audience feel nervous. Fortunately, Tung Wah was more skilled and ultimately eliminated Western Police with a score of 6-4, securing a spot in the semi-finals. Currently, in the Scotto Cup semi-final week, the French Business and Lax teams have already been decided. Yesterday, Lao Yi Er also eliminated Western Business with a score of 3-2, advancing with Tung Wah, still forming the top four powerhouses in the league. This truly adheres to the law of survival of the fittest. Let's see who will ultimately hold the reins this year. The starting lineups for both sides yesterday were as follows:

Tung Wah Association

Zhang Rongcai

Zhuang Youren, Li Yichen

Gu Shangrang, Feng Yunyou, Chen Zhenhe

Wanxianghua, Luo Haiguang, Dai Linjing, Sun Jinshun, Jia Youliang

Western Police Team

Mei En

Turner, Douglas

Han Lai, Ga Xu, Hui Sihe

Wei Li, Te Fei, Jack, Pei Te, Ao Ke Lai

Turner's Own Goal Allows Tung Wah to Score First

The two teams faced off. Tung Wah launched a central attack, but it was intercepted. Western Police's Ao Ke Lai dribbled the ball forward and safely passed it to the center. Te Fei lost his footing and kicked the ball out of bounds. After a brief pause, Western Police fouled again, and Li Yichen lost his footing, almost causing a disaster. Fortunately, Wei Li's shot was weak, missing the goal by just a few inches. Tung Wah launched a major counterattack. Wanxianghua charged forward with speed and precision, clearly visible. However, Mei En was tall and caught the ball with both hands. At this time, the ball was still circling in Western Police's defensive zone. Luo Haiguang chipped the ball into the center, and Sun and Jia made several short passes, showing great agility. When Jia passed the ball back to the center, Sun was a step too slow, and the effort fell short at the last moment, which was a pity. Western Police then seized the opportunity to advance. Pei Te charged forward alone, only five yards from the goal. Zhuang Youren rushed back to defend, blocking the shot and knocking it out of bounds. From the start until now, the two sides had been stalemated for twenty minutes, with neither side scoring. The audience was also uneasy. When Xianghua took a corner kick, Turner headed the ball, but it backfired, resulting in an own goal. Tung Wah scored first without effort.

Western Police Leads 3-2 in the First Half

The joy had barely passed when misfortune struck again. Western Police's center forward, Jack, received passes from both sides and shot from within the penalty area. Zhang Rongcai was momentarily distracted, and his diving save came too late. One goal was gained and one was lost, with only one minute separating the two. At twenty-four minutes, Tung Wah's offensive was strong when Western Police's right back, Douglas, violently tackled Wanxianghua inside the penalty area. Wan was injured and left the field. A penalty was awarded, and Dai Linjing took the shot. It went over the crossbar and out of bounds. Fortunately, Mei En moved before Dai had even stepped up, and a retake was ordered. Linjing confidently scored, putting them ahead again. Having lost a winger, Tung Wah felt restricted. Ao Ke Lai launched an attack. Sun Jinshun intercepted him midway, but Ao broke through again. Zhuang Youren hesitated for a moment, and Ao calmly scored, tying the game again at 2-2. After thirty-one minutes, Ao Ke Lai returned to the same spot and Zhuang Youren made a mistake, Zhang Rongcai stood in the wrong position, and Ao scored again. After this, the two sides remained stalemated for a long time without any progress. The first half ended with this score, with Western Police leading 3-2.

Tung Wah Association Reverses the Defeat to Win 6-4

After the lemon break, Wanxianghua returned to the field with an injury, and Tung Wah's strength doubled. Not long after the second half started, Tung Wah faced a dangerous situation but safely overcame it and immediately launched a counterattack. Sun and Jia advanced together, and Luo Haiguang's shot hit the post, another missed opportunity. Time flew by, and twenty-four minutes had passed in a flash. With Ga Xu directing the midfield for Western Police, the front line became active again. Wei Li led the attack, and Ao Ke Lai lay in ambush near the goalpost. He received the ball and gently shot, making it 4-2 to Western Police, causing the audience to feel dejected. Tung Wah's entire team was indignant. Jia Youliang launched a counterattack and shot, hitting He Lei in the body. Ga Xu staged another own goal, making it 3-4. Four minutes later, Western Police was offside. Chen Zhenhe took a free kick, Wanxianghua stepped forward and crossed the ball, and Dai Linjing caught up and scored, tying the game at 4-4. Western Police's offensive continued, and Tung Wah tried to trap them twice, but both of Ao Ke Lai's shots missed by inches. At thirty-six minutes, Zhuang Youren tackled and collided with a player, resulting in a penalty. With little time left, the outcome depended on this moment, making everyone sweat. Fortunately, Te Fei's shot was poor, hitting Rongcai's arms, averting the danger. Two minutes later, Turner blocked the ball with his arm, and Li Yichen took the penalty, but the ball flew high into the sky. Fortunately, three minutes later, they got another chance for a penalty. Sun Jinshun lived up to expectations and scored, determining the outcome of the game with only four minutes remaining. Unexpectedly, Dai Linjing added icing on the cake, scoring another goal one minute later, thus eliminating Western Police with a score of 6-4.

Continuous Intense Battles Lead to Fatigue; Jinan Unexpectedly Loses to Shakol; Russians Win 5-1; Jinan Relies Entirely on Penalty Kicks. 152

Jinan and Shakol met again yesterday at Shen Garden for the first match of the second round of the Shanghai League A Group. Jinan had been engaged in intense battles for several consecutive days, especially the match against Guanghua the day before, which was crucial for the University League championship and required their full effort. With many injured players, the soldiers were exhausted. Moreover, with both the A Group and Reserve Group matches scheduled yesterday, they lacked replacements. The soldiers took to the field with injuries to face the tall and fast Shakol. With different levels of rest, the outcome was immediately apparent. The Soviet army scored two goals within ten minutes through Boro Ning and Kai Rong Wei Wei District, making it 2-0 and causing Jinan to lose heart. Jinan tried hard to advance, but ultimately lacked strength in their kicks, and good opportunities were lost. The first half ended with a score of 2-0. In the second half, Jinan's offensive became stronger. Chen Pengze, Wang Nanzhen, and Wu Shufen successively shot at the goal, but all missed by millimeters. Guan Zhiyang and Chen Chunxi also repeatedly defended against the enemy's siege. After twenty minutes of stalemate, Merlin Noffsky attacked alone, avoided a pass to the center, and Holololov rushed to chip the ball. Ye Peichu blocked it with his right hand, but due to his short stature, the ball slipped into the net. Soon after, Holololov received a corner kick from the left wing, shot low, Ye leaned down to catch it, but due to the excessive force, the ball bounced in again. At this time, Soviet Shakol had already scored four goals, while Jinan had nothing. Soon after, the Soviet army's left back committed a handball foul, and Shi Yongnan scored the penalty, finally breaking the duck egg record. The momentum gradually improved, and good opportunities came in succession, but ultimately due to fatigue, every crucial moment was lost due to weak kicks. With ten minutes left in the game, the Soviet army's right wing suddenly attacked, turned to the left wing, Kai Luo Lie District passed the ball to the center, Merlin Noffsky arrived just in time and shot fiercely.
