The Truth About Central Government Finances in Recent Years 169

— Zhang Yifan

(1) Introduction

Since the establishment of the Republic, there has indeed been considerable progress in central government finances. For example, the financial report for the 23rd year of the Republic is now published. This is an obligation that the government of a democratic nation owes to its people. Without it, it cannot be said to serve the people, nor can it be said to be accountable to the people. However, this was impossible in the era of financial secrecy under the former Beijing government.

However, based on the statements in the previous reports, what we urgently want to understand is: What are the causes and effects of the massive expansion of today's revenues and expenditures? Where is the progress compared to the past? And what is the extent of that progress? Increased tax revenue does not necessarily indicate progress in the tax system. And an expanded expenditure cannot be simply concluded to be the result of political progress. There is no doubt that today's politics have advanced rapidly compared to the past, but is it indeed in line with economic principles? It seems that there is a need for review.

Speaking only of finance within the scope of finance, to what extent has the efficiency of financial administration been achieved? What is the impact of reorganizing the tax system, executing the budget, allocating finances, and providing public and private economic influence? The most ideal finance should not take "collection" as the basis of revenue for the public economy, but must be able to "produce" by itself to accumulate wealth, without competing with the people for profit, which is the best policy. However, very few countries in the world are able to do so. Our country, which is undergoing renewal, cannot immediately harbor such extravagant hopes. However, good finance must at least have a balance of income and expenditure. And it is not enough to just balance income and expenditure, it is necessary to ensure that every single penny of income and expenditure can have a good relationship with the people, both directly and indirectly. Therefore, after "taking from the people," it must be "used for the people"; and consideration should also be given to how to "take" and how to "use." The necessary rationality of the "taking" and "using" relationship is not only what the people of the whole country eagerly hope for, but also what the current authorities have set as a policy guideline, so our exploration should adhere to this point. Moreover, in this extraordinary period, if adjustments are not made quickly, so that "taking" conforms to the principle of minimizing sacrifice, retaining the flexibility of free elasticity, and "using" conforms to the principle of maximizing welfare, while being truly fully economical and fully rational, and has the function of adapting to extraordinary circumstances and completing extraordinary missions, and can ensure the natural development of public and private economies, and establish a sound foundation for peacetime response, then how can we talk about "saving the nation and seeking survival"?

The main purpose of this article is to explore the truth about central government finances in recent years, and the current state of its "taking" and "using" relationship. Therefore, it focuses on the organization and analysis of materials, and examines the process of development and the distribution of external influences. It does not indulge in empty talk, nor does it intend to make judgments. And it takes the narrow sense of finance as the scope. The figures cited are all based on the Financial Yearbook, Economic Yearbook, and successive accounting reports (all official figures), as well as the Shenbao Yearbook, and Shi Shiyi's "Financial History of the Republic of China" and its sequels, cross-referenced, selectively chosen, and recompiled and recalculated to discover the actual figures for "taking" and "using." Therefore, the results obtained are quite different from the publicly announced figures. This is because the publicly announced figures are mainly based on the net amount of direct revenue and expenditure of the national treasury, while what we want to pay attention to is the total amount of all revenue and expenditure of the national treasury, both directly and indirectly. This is why this article is titled "The Truth." As the public announcement is being made, it is believed that the people of the country are also happy to conduct further inspection. Therefore, may I take advantage of the valuable space of this publication to share it with like-minded people. Due to the author's limited talent and knowledge, errors are inevitable. I still hope that enlightened scholars will teach me!

(2) The Surge of Financial Expansion

Since the establishment of the National Government, the central government's expenditure has expanded year by year, which is a well-known fact. When the budget for the 16th year of the Republic was implemented, the final amount of expenditure was only 148 million yuan. However, in this year (the 25th year of the Republic), the budgeted amount of expenditure has soared to 991 million yuan. If the 16th year of the Republic is taken as the base year for the index, then the index for this year is 669.6; that is, it has increased sharply by 570%; in other words, it has increased sharply by more than five times. The average annual expenditure for the past ten years is calculated as 603 million yuan; enough to cover the total expenses of the past four or five years. Indeed, the expenditure of the past three or four years is sufficient to cover the total expenditure of the past six or seven years. The average expenditure index for the past ten years has also reached 462.1%, which is more than three and a half times higher than before, which shows the expansion of expenditure.

Since expenditure has expanded dramatically, revenue must also be increased strongly. Those who manage finances believe that the reason why public economy is not the same as private economy is that the former is "determining income based on expenditure," while the latter is "determining expenditure based on income."

In the 16th year of the Republic, the central government was still mainly located in the Jiangnan area; therefore, the final amount of revenue was only 80 million yuan (limited to normal revenue such as tax revenue; income from loans, etc. was excluded); later, the provinces revolted, and the country was formally unified, and huge subsidies were paid to exchange for the promotion and centralization of financial administration power. This exchange may not be a real problem in terms of national treasury revenue and expenditure, but it is what should be in terms of financial system. For a unified country, to build a modern country, the unification and centralization of financial power is the most basic requirement. With the unification and centralization of financial power, the annual revenue increased day by day; but because there was no real benefit to speak of, and the expansion of expenditure was as described above, it was necessary to work hard to increase tax rates and open up new sources of revenue. If the revenue amount of the 16th year of the Republic is taken as 100, then the average index for the past ten years has soared to 789.3; that is, the average increase is 689.3%; which is even greater than the increase rate of expenditure. If this year is compared with the 16th year of the Republic, then the increase rate has reached 862%. That is, it has increased more than eight and a half times compared to ten years ago.

Although the annual increase rate of revenue is greater than the increase rate of expenditure, the absolute figure, that is, the annual amount of revenue, is far less than the annual amount of expenditure. The average annual revenue for the past ten years is only 566 million yuan. The year with the largest revenue is only 770 million yuan. However, compared with the revenue amount of only tens of millions of yuan ten years ago, it has indeed increased sharply by six or seven times; and compared with the average annual expenditure of 635 million yuan over the years, the annual deficit is still as high as more than 100 million yuan on average. This deficit alone is almost enough to cover the entire expenditure of any year ten years ago.

Not only that, the deficit has become a normal state of our country's finance; there is no year without exception. And the amount of the deficit is increasing year by year. If the 16th year of the Republic is taken as the base year for the index, then the index for this year has reached 326.5; that is, it has increased by 226.5% compared to ten years ago; the average deficit index for the past ten years is 213%; that is, it has increased by 113% on average compared to before. Take a look at the first table - Annual Central Government Revenue and Expenditure Final Amount and its Index (unit: million yuan)

(Note) (1) The years from the 6th to the 14th year of the Republic are the era of the Beijing Government. The final amount of expenditure is based on the average annual amount of the total of military, political, and debt expenses directly paid by the Accounting Department of the Ministry of Finance and the Guan Yan Two Departments at that time. (2) The years from the 14th to the 15th year of the Republic are the era of the National Government of Guangdong and Wuhan: the following are the years since the establishment of the Nanjing National Government. Revenue and expenditure are all final figures, but the most recent two years are estimated figures. (3) The expenditure items include political debts and various expenses, and also include the collection fees directly used, which were removed from the previous reports, the amount owed from the previous year and paid in this year, and various temporary accounts; in the 17th year of the Republic, there were also various refunds. All are calculated together, and the remaining balance is deducted to show the actual expenditure of the national treasury. (4) The revenue items include tax revenue and income from state-owned business investments, etc., and also include the collection fees directly used, which were deducted in the previous public announcements; and deduct the income from debt funds and other temporary revenue, and the revenue owed from this year, etc. to clarify the actual revenue of the national treasury. (5) The deficit is based on the remainder after deducting the revenue amount from the expenditure amount. Therefore, the debt income amount is also included.

In the past, when talking about a balanced budget, it was always said to "increase revenue and reduce expenditure." Looking back at the sharp increase in revenue over the years, it can be seen that "straightening out tax revenue" and finding ways to "increase revenue" have indeed achieved remarkable results. However, the increase rate of revenue is 327% greater than the increase rate of expenditure, and the result is still not enough to maintain income balance; which is enough to indicate the weakness of the inherent poverty of the people's tax-paying ability.

Indeed: the people's tax-paying ability is originally composed of the possessions and income of China, and the increase or decrease of possessions and income is the result of the prosperity or decline of the national economy. Therefore, the financial foundation must be built on a sound national economy in order to maintain it without decay. However, the merits of the financial system and the influence of financial activities are also sufficient to dominate the rise and fall of the national economy. Because the two are indeed related to each other, we need to study the internal weaknesses of the strengthening of financial panic over the years.

(3) The Effect of Revenue Enhancement Plans Over the Years

According to a review of the budgets of various years since the 18th year of the Republic, compared with the final accounts; on the revenue side, the actual receipts are always more than 10% less than the budgeted amount. This phenomenon can be interpreted in two ways: one is that due to the excessive expansion of expenditure, the revenue budget amount has to be overestimated in order to reduce the large deficit on the budget paper. The second is that perhaps under each new revenue enhancement plan, the hope is fully estimated, but the result always fails to meet expectations. This fact is enough to illustrate the unbearable nature of the people's tax-paying ability; and from the financial standpoint, there is also a need for practical reform of the revenue enhancement plans over the years.

"Note, the revenue amount of the budget final accounts does not include debt income.

It goes without saying that tax revenue is the main body of our country's revenue, so all revenue enhancement plans over the years inevitably take the tax system as the sole target. It is also what is expected. Over the years, by "straightening out the tax system," things have been expanded: in terms of the increase in tax revenue, there has indeed been great progress. For example, the tax revenue in the 18th year of the Republic was only 116 million yuan; in the 15th year of the Republic, it sharply increased to 680 million yuan. It has increased sharply by 63.5% in eight years. And the increase in the most recent four years has been even more drastic. The average annual tax revenue for the four years from the 18th to the 21st year of the Republic was 492 million yuan, that is, the average increase was 17.5% in four years. But in the four years from the 22nd to the 25th year of the Republic, its average annual tax revenue has sharply increased to 652 million yuan. The average increase was 56.6%.

The sharp increase in tax revenue is as described above, but its position in the total revenue amount is decreasing day by day. For example, the ratio of tax revenue to total revenue in the 18th year of the Republic was 76.6%; in the 21st year of the Republic, it even increased to 79.9%: the average ratio for these four years was 75.2%. However, in the following four years, its average ratio has decreased to 69.9%; for example, in the 23rd year of the Republic, it was only 66.7%; and in the 25th year of the Republic, it was only 68.8%. This phenomenon is enough to illustrate that relying solely on the method of increasing taxes is far from enough to cope with the demand for a largely expanding expenditure, as shown in the third table:

Not only that, the so-called "straightening out the tax system" over the years is nothing more than strictly cracking down on smuggling, increasing tax rates, or opening up new tax sources. In terms of the financial principles of taxation, is it in line with economics? It is still a question. Not to mention its impact on the national economy. Take a look at the sharp increase in financial expenses since the 18th year of the Republic, its momentum is no less than the increase rate of tax revenue. As shown in the fourth table. (unit: million yuan)

From this, it can be seen that the average financial expenses have increased by 31.5% in the past eight years; indeed, in the salt affairs, due to the occupation of the Northeast salt administration by the Japanese puppet regime, the active organization of salt fields in the interior, the addition of salt police, the construction of warehouses, and the strict crackdown on smuggling have resulted in the largest increase in its expenses, reaching as high as 74%. Although the Northeast customs administration was also occupied, its expenses also increased by 21%. In terms of consolidated tax, due to the recent increase in new tax sources, the collection and grazing fees have also increased greatly. The average increase in the past eight years is 38.5%. In addition to these three major taxes, the administrative expenses of other taxes such as mining tax, stamp duty, and tobacco and alcohol tax have also increased across the board. The administrative expenses of mining tax were only 26,000 yuan in the 18th year of the Republic; in the 25th year of the Republic, they sharply increased to 534,000 yuan. An increase of more than 19 times. The average increase rate in the past eight years has also been at the high peak of 110.13%. The administrative expenses of stamp duty, tobacco and alcohol tax were only 3.55 million yuan in the 18th year of the Republic, but in the 25th year of the Republic, they have increased to over 5.2 million yuan, an increase of 47%; the average increase rate in the past eight years is 54.31%, but its total effect of increasing financial expenses only makes the total tax revenue increase by an average of slightly more than 56%. In terms of each tax, the tax with the largest increase rate is also the mining tax. The average increase in the past eight years is 1248.76%, which is indeed the consolidated tax, with an average increase of 96.4%; followed by stamp duty, tobacco and alcohol tax; with an average increase of 41.09%; followed by salt tax, with an average increase of 32.5%. Customs duty has an average increase of 20%. Take a look at the fifth table (unit: thousand yuan)

In finance, a tax must be collected with low collection costs and high tax revenue in order to be in line with economic principles. However, looking at various taxes, except for the consolidated tax administrative expenses, which account for only 4% of the consolidated tax revenue on average, the others account for more than 10%. For example, the mining tax fee in the 20th year of the Republic accounts for as much as 28.68% of the tax revenue; the average ratio in the past eight years has also reached 16.91%; the stamp duty, tobacco and alcohol tax fee in the 22nd year of the Republic accounts for 19.02% of the revenue; the average ratio in the past eight years is over 17%. Salt affairs fee accounts for 12% of the revenue on average; customs fee accounts for 10.26% of the revenue on average. The total financial fee accounts for as much as 9.78% of the total tax revenue on average. Although there has been a downward trend in recent years, the total tax revenue in the 25th year of the Republic will also be discounted by 195% due to the expenditure of financial fees. Take a look at the sixth table.

Percentage of tax affairs fees to the income of the tax itself

Note: Statistics based on the fourth and fifth tables. The ratio of financial expenses is to the total tax revenue.

Finance Minister Kong once said in the report of the 23rd year of the Republic, "For the tax collection agencies, either reorganize them or merge them, in order to save expenses and improve administration; since the implementation, it has been quite effective. The financial administrative fee has been reduced compared to before, and compared with tax revenue, its ratio was 11% in the 20th year, 9.9% in the 21st and 22nd year; and 9.2% in the 23rd and 24th year." The ratio seems to be still too low compared to what we have statistically calculated. However, this trend has indeed been formed. It cannot be said that this is the progress of financial administration today. However, looking back at the fourth table, today's austerity is still far from being comparable to the past, and it is hoped that the authorities can add more impetus.

Moreover, in terms of expenditure, the expenditure of financial fees is almost equal to the entire total amount of other administrative expenses; and sometimes it even exceeds it. The amount is only second to the military affairs and debt fees. It goes without saying that it is a major burden on finance. During this period of preparing for national defense and actively suppressing bandits, there is only concern that the military affairs fee cannot be increased, and there is no reason to reduce it again. The debt fee is related to national credit, and reserves the space to make up for future financial deficits, so it is also difficult to reduce it. Therefore, for the sake of balancing the budget and strengthening the finance, the only way is to reduce the administrative affairs fee and the financial fee. Reducing the political fee does not mean a general salary reduction, but in addition to salary reduction, we should also engage in cutting redundant officials and abolishing redundant posts; this will greatly contribute to the transformation of the administrative system and the increase of administrative efficiency.

Moreover, the expenditure of financial fees is actually equivalent to the entire nation paying taxes to provide for tax officials. The special fees of each tax are actually the additional tax levied on each tax. Today, 9.78% of the country's total tax revenue is the income from the additional tax levied for financial fees. Therefore, the larger the ratio of each tax affairs fee to the tax itself, the higher the tax rate of its additional tax. In order to relieve the people's difficulties and reduce the tax rate, we should first reduce this additional tax rate.

Not only that, today's increase in tax grazing is not the result of improved financial fees and increased administrative efficiency. Take the salt tax as an example.

In recent years, efforts have been spared to rectify the salt affairs. Rectifying salt fields, building warehouses, and widely setting up tax police have all increased salt affairs fees: and the purpose is to prevent smuggling and attempt to increase tax revenue. According to the fifth table, in the past eight years, salt tax revenue has increased by an average of 32.5%; but according to the fourth table, the expenditure of salt affairs fees has increased by an average of 74.1%. Paying twice the price and only getting one effect: it can be said that "doing more work with half the result." It is obvious that the gains do not make up for the losses. If the amount of smuggling fees is increasing year by year, and the national salt release is still very small, it can be said that its effect is weak. Take a look at the seventh table: (unit: million yuan and dan)

In the past eight years, the smuggling fee has increased by an average of 11 times: the salt release has only increased by 9.5%; spending 11 times the smuggling fee, only 9.5% of the smuggled salt has been confiscated into official salt. The average increase rate of salt tax is 29.5%: on the other hand, the salt tax rate has increased by 65.3%. It can be seen that the tax revenue progress rate is far less than the tax rate increase rate; and the great function of cracking down on smuggling may only prevent the new smuggled salt from evading tax due to the sharp increase in the tax rate. The price is so high, but the effect is only mediocre. It can be seen that increasing the tax rate and strictly cracking down on smuggling is obviously not a good idea. It is very obvious. This forecast is probably not unique to the salt tax.

Indeed, smuggling is originally a criminal act. If it were not for the excessive tax burden and the people's unbearable life, who would be willing to take the risk again? Salt is a daily necessity for everyone, and it is said that tax on it is a great source of wealth from a financial standpoint. If the country has 450 million people, and each person consumes 15 catties of salt per year, then the national annual salt release must be at least 67.5 million dan. If the tax rate implements the new salt law's regulations of 2.5 yuan per city ancestor; then the annual tax revenue can reach 163 million yuan. Once the tax rate is reduced, smugglers will be reduced; if more economical collection fees are used to reform transportation and sales and crackdown on smuggling, and fully improve their administrative efficiency, then the financial benefits obtained will be more than today; and the burden on people's lives will be greatly reduced.

Moreover, the benefits and harms of taxation on people's lives are like double-edged swords. Its right edge can destroy the national economy and dry up the tax source; its left edge can help the national economy and cultivate the national financial resources. Therefore, whether it is a disaster or a blessing depends on how to use its edge.

(4) Changes and Expectations in the Content of Expenditure

As mentioned earlier, in the past ten years, the central government's expenditure has increased by an average of more than three and a half times. In the past, the largest increase rate was in the three categories of military affairs, finance, and debt expenses. However, since the 22nd year of the Republic, the content with the largest increase has changed. Economic administrative expenses, cultural education expenses, administrative judicial expenses, subsidies, etc. are all increasing rapidly. This change is indeed a sign of great progress in the central government's finances compared to the past. Is it not also a manifestation of being stimulated by national disasters? Take a look at the eighth table

Final Accounts of Various Expenditures and Their Indices and Ratios (unit: thousand yuan)

"Note" (1) The Beijing government era includes the 2nd, 3rd, 5th, 8th, and 14th years of the Republic; the above numbers are the total average of the estimated averages for those four years (2) Subsidies include Mongolian and Tibetan expenses in the mountains, (3) Financial expenses in the Beijing era also included debt expenses. (4) Cultural and education expenses, formerly known as education expenses, or expenses in charge of the Ministry of Education (5) Economic administrative expenses, including transportation, industry, private establishment, and state-owned capital investment. In the past, they included agriculture, commerce, transportation, and industry. In the 18th year of the Republic, there were also items such as industry and commerce, agriculture and mining, and health. (6) Administrative judicial expenses, including former foreign affairs, internal affairs, and judicial affairs; or expenses of various agencies. Today, they include state affairs expenses, internal affairs expenses, judicial affairs expenses, foreign affairs expenses, and pension expenses. (7) The ratio is obtained by calculating each expense against the total expenditure of the current year. (8) The index is based on the 18th year of the Republic.

National taxpayers believe that the purpose of fulfilling their due obligations is not entirely to maintain the administrative organization of the country, but to obtain guarantees of life, property, and all business and life, and to have full convenience for improvement and development. The country also has the right to levy taxes on the people based on this contribution. Regardless of the origin of the country and its realistic essence, it is not like this. However, modern political thought all takes this as a guideline. Therefore, the country's levy of taxes must conform to the principle of minimizing sacrifice and maximizing welfare. And the country's use of tax money must also conform to the principle of minimizing sacrifice and maximizing welfare; in other words: a good tax system makes the people feel less sacrificed when paying taxes and can expect the greatest welfare. The country then spends the tax money collected at the lowest cost, in order to maintain and create the greatest public welfare; and fulfill its due responsibilities to the people. In this way, society can prosper and move upward, and the foundation of the country can be strengthened and consolidated. Finance can also be maintained without fatigue. Therefore, the nature of the country's revenue is only the circulation of wealth, and the nature of expenditure is actually equal to intangible or tangible production investment. The greater the amount of tangible production investment, the more sound the financial foundation and the greatest welfare created. Therefore, the allocation of expenditure funds is the key to the merits of the national political system.

Looking at the various expenditures of the country over the years, in the past nine years, military expenses have accounted for an average of 40.29% of the total expenditure; debt expenses have accounted for 32.05%; the two together account for 72.34%. Subsidies, most of which actually have the nature of military expenses, account for an average of 6.23%. Then the total is 78.57%. Financial expenses, administrative judicial expenses, and party affairs expenses can be collectively called political expenses. The average ratio of these over the past nine years is 13.04%. The above-mentioned expenses, as they are now, are essentially no different from pure consumption. The other two expenses are more active in production, but their ratio is only 8.54% in total.

However, since the 22nd year of the Republic, military expenses have decreased by 36.55%; the average ratio in the past four years has decreased by 37.98%. Although the absolute amount of debt expenses has decreased little, the average ratio has decreased to 27.5%. Subsidies, during this period, have increased sharply by 532.8%. Its average ratio is 8.63%. The ratio of the three combined has decreased to 74.11%.

During this period, although the absolute amount of financial expenses has also decreased little, the ratio has decreased to 7.17%; the absolute amount of administrative judicial expenses has increased sharply by 49.6%; but its average ratio is still only 3.69%. Because this expense was very small in the past, a slight increase, although very small in the total largely expanding expenditure, in the vertical comparison, it has been felt that its progress is fast. If party affairs expenses are added, the average ratio of these three expenses in this period has also decreased to 11.47%.

However, cultural education and economic administration expenses have all increased sharply in this period. The former's absolute amount has increased by 198%; the average ratio has expanded to 3.5%; the latter's absolute amount has increased sharply by 1648.6%; the average ratio has increased and expanded to 11%. The average ratio of the two combined during this period is 14.5%. The rate of increase in the absolute amount is faster than the expansion of the average ratio, for the same reason as the increase in administrative judicial expenses.

In terms of the responsibilities of the state, whether it is culture, laws and regulations, education, or defense, they should be actively organized. Indeed, in our country, everything has been abandoned, and we should advance simultaneously and carry out practical consolidation. However, in this time of people's poverty and financial exhaustion, and with internal and external troubles, it is impossible to do everything at once. Therefore, weighing the importance and choosing the key points to proceed first is a necessary path. Then we can celebrate greatly for the fact that the center of gravity of expenditure is changing.

However, from the financial point of view, we cannot help but feel new worries about today's changes. Precisely because the people are impoverished and the country is financially exhausted, every move should adhere to economic principles. We cannot waste money because of popular support, make finance an unsustainable expansion, and fall into greater panic. Or, for the convenience of various agencies in carrying out affairs, expand the scale, add organizations, and hire personnel, creating a situation where officials are more than jobs, and jobs are abandoned due to the mutual constraints of various related agencies: things are limited by financial consumption in the salary expenditures of redundant officials and supervisors. This disrupts the complete administrative system, reduces the efficiency of administration, and wastes national treasury, strengthening the financial crisis. Unfortunately, this phenomenon occurs frequently in economic administration.

When He Lian studied the issue of adjusting the central administrative organization today (his paper was published in the Nankai University Journal of Political Economy, Volume 4, Issue 3), he listed in detail the complexity and confusion of the central administrative organizations, and strongly stated its impropriety. And he believed that the economic administration's multitude of agencies and divided responsibilities were very serious. It can be seen that in this rapidly expanding economic administration fee, a large part must be the expenditure of salary for redundant officials and supervisors. Therefore, in order to improve administrative efficiency, we should adjust the administrative structure; in order to balance the budget, save waste, and supplement reasonable expenditure, we should also adjust the administrative structure, as a means to practice the promise of "reducing expenditure."

"Five" The Impact of the Expansion of Revenue and Expenditure on Finance

The sharp increase in normal revenue is not enough to meet the demand for a largely expanding expenditure. The amount of the annual deficit in the national treasury is also so huge. Therefore, the means to balance the budget is only to issue national debt and allocate credit.

According to Finance Minister Kong's report, the recent sharp increase in national debt is "mostly used to repay old debts"; and he also said that "the shortfall of each year can be largely offset by the expenditure of repaying debts." This is indeed a faithful explanation of borrowing to repay debts.

Not only that, the amount of debt repaid over the years is not as large as the amount of new debt issued. Because not only is issuing new debt a means to make up for the budget deficit, but also all unreceived tax money is converted into treasury bills or loans to pay for urgently needed money. In the past ten years, an average of 319 million yuan of new debt has been issued annually; almost equal to the total expenditure of the past two or three years ten years ago. The amount of debt raised is greater than the amount of debt repaid and the deficit, which is more dangerous than "borrowing to repay debts." Finance Minister Kong's report also said that "The newly issued bonds are issued at a discount to the face value, so the actual interest is extremely high. And the national tax revenue that has been designated as the guarantee for the new debt is also increasing day by day." It is truly the suffering that can only be imagined by those who have personally experienced it. Take a look at the ninth table:

(Note) Unit: million yuan, the number before the 23rd year is the final account, and the number after is the estimated amount. New debt includes domestic and foreign debt, loans and outstanding amounts, and debt rolling includes industrial bonds; the rolling amount of this year is as of the end of March, and is calculated by year. The new debt of this year includes the sum of the amount reduced annually by 85 million yuan in debt fees by the central government due to the issue of reunification bonds, rehabilitation, and Sichuan relief.

According to this, it can be known that the annual increase rate of debt is at least 12.1% higher than the previous year; the highest increase rate is as high as 224.2%, as in this year. Its average increase rate is 56%. In the past ten years, the issue increase rate is 443.3%; the debt rolling amount increase rate is 596.1%; ten years later, the rolling amount of national debt will surely exceed 10 billion yuan. The increased issuance and circulation of national debt can indeed promote currency inflation. (Please see the fourth section of my humble book in the Social Economic Monthly Report, Volume 3, Issue 7 for the reason) According to the China Bank report, "The amount of securities held by national banks is equal to the amount of paid-in capital of national banks; and even exceeds it," and these securities are all government bonds. Furthermore, the means for banks to bear government bonds often rely on increasing their paper money issuance, and those with capital often convert it into money after receiving government bonds; the country pays the income occupied by the government to the people, and then increases the people's deposits in banks. Increased deposits help to increase currency issuance. Currency circulation is attacked by panic, and then condenses into interest-seeking capital. As a result, the cash reserve ratio only decreases and does not increase. The circulation of currency will all be transformed into book assets. Therefore, the actual benefits of expansion have not been obtained, but the foundation of expansion has been formed. The double threat of debt interest and commodity prices makes the expansion of financial expenditure endless. In addition to paying taxes to the state, the people must also pay taxes to the state's creditors.

However, today's gradual change in expenditure, shifting its focus to economic administration and engaging in productive investment, has enabled finance to reap considerable benefits. In recent years, in addition to the two major incomes of tax revenue and debt funds, the income from state-owned enterprises and investment profits has also gradually increased. If the authorities can move forward with this new policy, the financial foundation should have hope of turning danger into safety. Take a look at the tenth table: Analysis of the content of revenue over the years.

(Note) Other income includes income from state-owned railways, interest income from bank official shares, and the revenue owed from this year.

The above table shows that in the past seven years, although tax revenue has occupied the highest position in revenue, its increase rate is the lowest. Only increasing year by year, except when the 918 Incident and the recent armed smuggling trend in North China occurred, there was an exceptional decline. But by strengthening tax revenue in other areas, the loss was compensated for: therefore, the decline rate was not large. Debt funds occupy the second highest position in revenue, but its ratio, like tax revenue, has a downward trend. However, other income, which was negligible in revenue in the past, has become increasingly important in recent years. Although it includes the revenue owed, making it difficult for us to draw conclusions. But in general, it is not impossible for revenue items to also have a changing situation. This is exactly what we are looking forward to. Two five, one one, three zero, evening

Yarn and Cotton: Purchase American Cotton on Price Dips 173

Yesterday, American cotton opened. Due to profit-taking by bulls at home and abroad, uncertainties in British politics, the upcoming government report, and weekend selling pressure, as well as the uncertainty of the government management law in New Orleans, October contracts were sold off, with prices falling two to six points per pound. Traders purchased on price dips. Currently, cotton is firm, while the cloth market is relatively slow. At closing, there was some buying, and the market situation was stable. Spot prices fell eight points per pound, while futures prices fell three to eight points per pound. British cotton spot prices fell one point, while futures prices remained unchanged. Indian cotton initially rose due to purchases by mainland merchants and exporters, and short covering, but later fell due to profit-taking by bulls. Pingguo'er fell 0.25 rupees, Aomula rose 0.25 to 0.5 rupees, and Bairoxi rose 0.5 rupees. The original telegram is recorded on the left. (5th dispatch)

According to a dispatch from Bombay, the opening forecast for the 7th is: Bairoxi at 210.5 rupees, down 0.5 rupees; Aomula at 197.5 rupees, down 0.75 rupees; Pingguo'er at 160 rupees, down 0.5 rupees.

Tidbits 177

— (Fang Shujun)

"Obstacles" are our sharpest weapons for advancement. The happiness of a person lies in discovering and removing obstacles. Because an obstacle blocks one's ambition, it inevitably gives rise to a kind of courage to overcome it. The greater the obstacle, the fiercer one's courage and the more one strives for progress; otherwise, one is a mediocre person.

"If one does not exert oneself, one will inevitably become decadent; if one does not restrain oneself, one will inevitably become licentious." These words of Zhu Xi are the experience. If we want to be self-reliant, self-strengthening, and self-helping in the world, we must endure hardship and work hard to move forward. Wounds and overturns, thorns and reefs are not enough to hinder our progress.

Make the world powers realize that we Chinese men are lions and not sheep." These are the words of Mr. Luo Jialun comforting and encouraging the Suiyuan soldiers. At this time of national crisis and ethnic peril, we should fully strive for the country and the nation, embracing the spirit of struggle and the determination to sacrifice, and take on the heavy responsibility of "wielding weapons to defend the country." Only then can the mountains and rivers of our great Chinese nation, dyed red with blood, be possessed by us.

Xu Guqing's Proficiency in Literature 178

— Sun Choucheng

Mr. Xu Guqing, who died of illness in Shanghai on September 13 of this year, was once the commander of the Ninth Division of the Army in the late Qing Dynasty. During the Xinhai Revolution, he attacked Ning and was promoted as the commander-in-chief of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Allied Forces. He followed the Prime Minister south to uphold the Constitution and served as the commander-in-chief of the Guangzhou Garrison and concurrently supervised troop training. Therefore, people all thought he was a brave warrior. Unexpectedly, Mr. Xu was not born in the army. In his youth, his father, Mr. Ziyuan, was a classics teacher and a famous secretary. He was well-read and versatile. He received his family education and studied diligently, researching the learning of the Song Confucians. At the age of nineteen, he was hired by Huaiyuan County as a criminal secretary. After work, he studied classics, gathered disciples, established learning societies, and taught diligently. He also studied medicine extensively and often treated his own illnesses. He also passed the imperial examination in the Jiazi year of the Guangxu era and entered the staff of Governors Zhang Guangyu and Li Mianlin of Guilin. When Li Mianlin was promoted to Governor of Jiangxi, he followed him to Jiangxi and entered officialdom. As a Daoist, he assisted Li in investigating the Jiangxi religious cases and concluded more than 2,000 cases in three months. Therefore, he was praised for his ability and was appointed as the head of the Military Academy and the chief of camp affairs, leading the new army. At that time, Mr. Xu resigned because he was not familiar with military affairs. Governor Li asked him to use the learning of Laozi to govern the army, believing that he would be invincible. He once said that it was easy to get a famous general, but difficult to find a Confucian general, and asked him not to resign. From then on, he was in charge of military affairs wherever he went, and his literary talent was buried. In addition to being the general manager of the Camp Affairs Office in Jiangxi, he commanded the standing army in Guangdong, and he was the chief of the Military Affairs Bureau in Fujian. In Jiangnan, he was the chief of the Staff and Training Office, and he also commanded the standing army. He personally drafted the regulations for the new army's organization and the model orders, and he handled the micro-soldiers. Many of the generals in his department had revolutionary ideas, such as Zhao Boxian, who died in Huanghuagang, Xiong Chengji, who died in the uprising in Anhui, and Bai Wenwei, who filled the position of Governor of Anhui. At that time, they were all under his command. Governor Duan Fang of Jiangxi named them for arrest, but he rescued them and escaped. Recently, he served as a member of the National Government, but due to illness, he often recuperated in Shanghai, calling himself the Old Man of Learning and Longevity, and wrote books such as the Anthology of Learning and Longevity Hall, Poetry Theory, and Poetry Collection for his own entertainment.

Street of Terror 179

— Rongyu

XXX Road has long been known as the "Street of Mystery" because it has foreign girls selling their bodies; it also has domestic men and women doing secret plays that are harmful to customs and shocking to hear; in addition, cafes, dance halls, gambling dens, opium dens... also have special scenery, so it has won that mysterious emblem. However, since the "January 28th" Incident, the depression of the market and the strict crackdown by the police and patrol rooms have made these mysterious activities less rampant than before. Therefore, the name "Street of Mystery" is somewhat unworthy of the name.

Last year and this year, two international assassination cases occurred near this "Street of Mystery," and the assassinated people were brave warriors who held the important task of protecting overseas Chinese. "Zhang Tianshi was bewitched by ghosts," and it was somewhat embarrassing on the surface. Therefore, on the one hand, they negotiated with the municipal government of this city; on the other hand, they demonstrated to the citizens. The XXX Road had a post every five steps and a sentry every ten steps, with real guns and live ammunition, knives unsheathed, tanks and machine cars constantly patrolling, and suddenly it was filled with a tense atmosphere. Residents living nearby had tasted the flavor of the "January 28th" night, so they fled! Fled! Fled to the center of the concession, fled to the countryside in the interior. The XXX Road suddenly became deserted, with nine out of ten houses empty and few pedestrians. Along the north side, fifteen out of ten shops were closed, and no longer could be heard the music of the dance hall, the noise of the sailors, and the laughter of the enchanting women. The people walking on the road were also full of worries, and if they were not careful, they would suffer the disaster of being a fish in the pond. The families living by the roadside should also be careful of fire, be cautious in everything. Dropping a longan pit or splashing a basin of washing water would not only violate the police regulations, but also face the danger of military law. The XXX Road, which has always been known as mysterious, has become known as the street of terror because the residents are trembling and the pedestrians are trembling.

The Eve of the Revolution 180

— Manzi

The history of the National Revolution is tragic. It is not long ago, and we are easily longing for it. But we want a deep remembrance. Although it is a rehash of old events, it is a very good history textbook.

"Life and Death Together" writes about the eve of the revolution, the brutality of the warlords, and the struggles of the revolutionary comrades. Of course, it is a painful historical trace. Director Ying Yunwei handled this imaginable story in a very sharp way, because he used all his strength to develop the tense emotions. Therefore, no one who has seen this film does not solemnly expect the development of the facts. For a full hour, they could not even breathe until the revolutionary army finally won and they could recover from the suffocation in the cheers. But the terror obtained may take more time to fade. Therefore, in the miasma of soft films, this is a film that rises suddenly from the army.

We don't need to associate it with the national defense issue, but national defense requires the people to sacrifice everything, and it requires the people to never give up. To encourage the people, there must be strong stimulation and excitement. "Life and Death Together" bears this mission, so in the final life-and-death juncture when the national crisis is serious, we should take "Life and Death Comrades" as a textbook for raising awareness and awakening. To put it bluntly, "Life and Death Comrades" is a reference book for national defense education.

We remember that the greatest help of the National Revolutionary Army was the propaganda work. "Life and Death Comrades" writes about the success of the propaganda work, and the setbacks encountered before the success are the different and similar types of the martyrs that the central government has successively commended. Then "Life and Death Comrades" can also be said to be a representative work of the Kuomintang Party history.

In terms of technology, Yuan Muzhi can play two roles at the same time, and he can take care of the plot without being stiff or abrupt. In terms of the personality of two different people, he can use the reflection ability to the extreme. Chen Bo'er also showed the self-awareness of women. Today's new women should be like this. Yun Guangzhao, a humorous hero, has small actions in his solemn performance, which are like a smiling star shining in the dark clouds when it is raining.

High Pillow 181

— Fan Xianwei

The common saying "sleep high and worry-free" originally described a group of people who spent their years leisurely, "worry-free about clothes" and "worry-free about food," but the high pillow I am talking about now is not like this. In the past, it really made a big splash, sleeping publicly for many years, and sleeping on it was indeed carefree and out of the dust! However, now that the times have changed, this kind of high pillow can no longer be slept on, and it has become a high pillow with worries. This high pillow, also known as the "smart pillow," is often slept on by opium addicts. The oil stains are at least two points high. When wheezing and snotting, they lie down and blow a few pipes, which stimulates their minds and makes them energetic. You can't think of difficult problems, and events that cannot be solved will be solved easily. It is truly a wonderful elixir!

In recent years, the government's prohibitions have become stricter and stricter. It is said that from next year, if anyone is caught sleeping on a high pillow privately, their head will be asked to move! What's more, this year has been a bottomless pit: thousands and hundreds of acres of good farmland, three-entry and four-beam halls, beautiful "wives" like flowers, and lively and delicate sons can be accommodated as much as possible, and the fancy banknotes are used up. In the end, they still have to be caught in the net of the law. What is the point! I advise the blacklisted compatriots to wake up quickly!

Some people say that one of the reasons why sports are not developed in China is that they like to sleep on high pillows. Indeed, the pillows we sleep on every day are at least half a foot high, so everyone is bent over and creating a large number of hunchbacks, the style is really modern! You must know that the higher the pillow, the more curved the back, so the lungs will naturally not be very developed, and the physique will not be strong again? This also makes sense, so not only opium addicts should not sleep on high pillows, but ordinary people are also unsuitable; even if they can't get rid of it, it is better to be lower!

Four Poems on General Su Bingwen's End-of-Year Sentiments 182

— Wu Zhuzhong

The national scourge has not ceased, and I only feel that the sleeping lion has awakened day by day. The mountains and rivers are stained with blood and tears, and heroes from all directions display their heroism. The chariots and horses are swift beyond the Great Wall, and the plants and trees in the battlefields are stained with the smell of killing thieves. Not asking what happened in those years, the general's ambition is so high that it reaches the blue sky.

The military orders are strict like frost and camps are set up on the ground. The sound of war drums rumbles for a hundred thousand Xiong Ba. I am willing to use iron and blood to quell the chaos of the times, and I do not care about my family or life and death. The flames of war spread and invade the Hu moon, and the victory or defeat of weapons is like a national chess game. The festering wounds are the heroic deeds of fierce battles, and the aura that conquers the city is like the pressure of a city.

In the tiger tent, the inkstone condenses and drafts are planned. Heroic ambition wants to sever the flow in the water. Carrying bits in their mouths, they trudge through the snow to chase the barbarians, and dance swords and fly frost to shoot at the Big Dipper. Wrapping the body in horsehide is a loyal promise to the country, and lying in the sand field and watching the moon is a laugh at being ennobled. Now that the lifelong wish has not been fulfilled, I will sweep away the evil spirits and be a companion with the ancients.

The moon is full in the lonely city and the saddle is not untied. Driving the chariot and horses at dawn and dusk. The generosity dyes the three borders red with blood, and the desolation urges the cold with snow for ten thousand miles. The voice of heaven has already moved the desert north, and my heart will be at peace when I return my rivers and mountains.

Replaced Luan and Phoenix 183

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 9: Hearing the Bad News, People Are Like Flowers Falling into the Cesspool, and the Fragrant Traces Are Frequent, and the Heart Is Like Catkins Sticking to Mud

After twelve o'clock, Guoqi felt that the messenger would not come again. After eating lunch, he picked up a book and flipped through a few pages at random, which only added another layer of annoyance to his heart. The slight wind shook the bamboo curtains outside the window non-stop. From that action, the long-drawn sound of cicadas came from afar, rustling. When the strong white light of the sun shone into the courtyard, listening to the sound of cicadas gave a feeling of a very long day, and people felt sleepy and drowsy. So he moved a rattan chair and lay down facing the window. He didn't know how long it had been when he heard a few knocks by his ear. When he opened his eyes, he saw half a flowered dress outside the door curtain. He immediately stood up and nodded to the outside and said: Is it Ms. Li? Please come in. As he said this, he quickly took down the long gown on the hook and wanted to put it on. Aunt Liu outside the door replied: Sir, it's me. Guoqi had already put on his long gown. It was not good to take it off again and asked: What are you doing knocking on my door? Aunt Liu smiled and said: I am nailing two nails on the wall. Guoqi said: But it's good that you woke me up, I was just about to go out. As he said this, he rubbed his eyes and was about to lift the curtain to go out. Aunt Liu saw it from the crack in the door curtain and said: Sir, are you going out? There is a guest at home. Guoqi said: What guest is at home? Aunt Liu said: Miss Li came a long time ago and is sitting in the old lady's room. She said she wanted to borrow a book from you. If you wake up, just call him. Guoqi smiled and said: You don't speak clearly, which makes me confused. Go and tell Miss Li that if she wants any books, just come and get them. I'll wait here, I won't go out. Saying this, he felt a special kind of happiness and forgot all about blaming Youmei for breaking her promise. He touched his collar and pulled his lapel, and didn't sit down, quietly waiting for Youmei to come in. But Youmei's attitude was very gentle. After more than ten minutes, he first called out cousin across the door curtain, and then slowly lifted the door curtain and came in. Probably because of the heat, he didn't comb his long braids, but tied a butterfly bun on the top of his head. He was wearing a long light blue foreign gauze jacket. Although he was a muscular person, he also showed a slender figure. I don't know if he had applied rouge on his face, but two blushes had already appeared on his cheeks. When he came in, he smiled slightly at Guoqi and bowed: Cousin, didn't you go out today? (106)

Special Feature

Greatly Spoiling the Scenery 184

— Yafei

As long as we think of the "January 28th" incident four years ago, none of us will forget Dachang, because Dachang and Miaohang were both important military locations at that time, so even now, the scars of the past catastrophe and the ruins after the war can still be seen everywhere.

At that time, I was also one of the survivors of the war, so for four or five years, that cruel and painful impression will never disappear from my memory; as long as I walk to those places, I will think of these things. Currently, the sound of cannons in Suiyuan is ringing again. The tricks that were performed in the south in the past have now been moved to the north in a different way. When we look back on the past, the new wounds and old pains all come to our hearts together.

On a day without sun, we were carried by the Shanghai-Tai long-distance bus, starting from Wuzhen Road Bridge, passing through Zhongxing Road, Taiyangmiao Road, Zhongshan Road, and finally climbing onto the long Shanghai-Tai Road; leaving the city and gradually moving towards nature. The rivers, farmhouses, and trees outside the car window retreated backwards like lightning.

When the car arrived at Dachang, we all got off in a crowd. It was the first time for all of us to come to Dachang, so we were not only unfamiliar with the route, but also a little unclear about the direction. But fortunately, we didn't have a specific destination, so we just let go of our steps and let our toes break through. We took a turn at the station, passed through an alley, and could see a cement bridge. That bridge was destroyed during the January 28th Incident and rebuilt by a gentleman's donation. Therefore, the bridge railings were all engraved with the cause of the destruction and the names of the donors. Walking down the bridge is Dachang Town.

Although the town market of Dachang is not very big, it is also quite prosperous, with taverns, sauce gardens, and firms. However, the town appearance does not seem to be very neat. We toured the street for a week and felt that the hotels and teahouses were not very deserted. After passing the town, a very high memorial archway stood at the end of the market, knowing that it was also built to commemorate the revitalization of the town.

Behind the town, there is a large farm. The farm covers an area of two or three hundred acres, with many seedlings and livestock types. Moreover, the shallow green lawns and the winding rivers are dotted with many pavilions, so although this is a farm, it also has the advantage of a garden. Especially in spring or summer, I believe that the living environment there must be very good!

Coming out of the farm, passing the security team headquarters, a group of team members were playing basketball. Behind the team headquarters, there is also a small garden, with a sign "Our Garden" erected on it.

Hearing the locals tell us that there is still an ancient Baohua Temple three or four miles away from the town, which is worth visiting. So we asked the locals for directions, and I arrived at Baohua Temple. The temple is indeed very large, with many monks, and it seems that the temple was rebuilt after the "January 28th" incident, so the houses still retain new traces. There are inscriptions by Mr. Wang Zhen, a native of Bailong Mountain, everywhere. Behind the temple, there is a courtyard, where there is a very large release pond and pavilions, as well as a river.

After visiting the temple, it was already dusk when I came back. But looking around the fields, I couldn't find my way home. Later, after passing through several field paths, I finally walked to Yuqing Bridge. I finally waited for the last Shanghai-Tai bus back to Shanghai at Yuqing Bridge and was taken back to Shanghai.

Supplementary Local Edition of Shen Bao

Commentary

Sai Jinhua is Dead 195

— Xin Xin

Sai Jinhua is dead.

Sai Jinhua was once prominent for a time. As the saying goes, "Her reputation filled the nine cities, and everyone began to praise Second Master Sai." Sai Jinhua not only used charm to win the favor of adults and gentlemen, but also used boldness to make people "praise" her. More than thirty years ago, under feudal forces, she dared to break the boundaries between men and women without any scruples, and this boldness was enough to stun the close-minded.

But because of this, she was seen by some adults and gentlemen as a "strange costume" flaunting in the streets. The monster that will lead to the demise of the country.

The "upright" adults regarded her as a "monster that would lead to the demise of the country," and the reason was very simple: all old things, when they are about to decline and there is no way to remedy their decline, they always envy, resent, and thus want to destroy all new things. The new things that they initially opposed and destroyed may have direct conflicts of interest with the old, but over time, because they feel that there are more and more new things and they are becoming stronger and stronger, destroying them is really beyond their ability and there is no way to destroy them, so they have to close their eyes and ignore how chaotic they are, and because the greater new forces are no longer something they can destroy, they have to choose the weak to attack. The reason why new clothes were ridiculed as "strange costumes" was not really because of their "strangeness," but because they were "new."

Therefore, although the "upright" adults regarded her as a "monster that would lead to the demise of the country," the masses sympathized with her. Their sympathy was not because the masses had higher insights than the adults and gentlemen, knowing that the demise of the country had nothing to do with "strange costumes," and they would never turn their thoughts to "strange costumes." It was really because her boldness and her behavior of daring to resist traditional ideas stunned them, and they felt her loveliness intuitively. Although the masses were cowardly and dared not show resistance under the heavy pressure of thousands of years, they did have a psychology of worshipping resisters.

As for the fact that some self-proclaimed romantic adults and gentlemen liked her, it was also somewhat similar to this point. She was a

Page 18

Charming woman, but she was different from other women who only knew how to be charming. Other women had nothing else besides obedient obedience, but she also had the spirit of youth and dared to express her lively temperament. Thus, after the general self-proclaimed romantic adults and gentlemen became tired of the sentimental Lin Daiyu-style women, they liked her because of her novelty and stimulation. What's more, she also had the titles of "Imperial Envoy's Wife" and "Top Scholar's Wife." Once there is a title, it has been an example from ancient times to the present that they are regarded as rare commodities. Just say now, aren't "Empress" and "Campus Belle" more valuable than ordinary ones?

Naturally, the masses' unforgettable memory of her is also for a greater reason. This reason is to copy a line from the "Sai Jinhua" script: "In this time of great national change, it is not the great officials and mansions who can really speak for the people, but such a beautiful girl!" Because "such a beautiful girl" saved their lives, while those great officials and mansions were at a loss. Even if the masses were worse off, they would always know who gave them benefits and who gave them harm. Although after Sai Jinhua did not get much benefit from the masses.

Sai Jinhua was one who was able to prolong her life in troubled times by accidentally taking the enemy's favor with her body. Because of this accidental opportunity, she was able to "sell a little face" and beg the enemy for mercy for the people. Moreover, because of the internal contradictions of the various imperialist powers, she was considered to have fulfilled a "meritorious service" that the ministers could not fulfill for Empress Dowager Cixi. (Please do not forget that this "meritorious service" was exchanged for twelve humiliating national treaties, including an indemnity of 450 million taels of silver and the prohibition of setting up military defenses on the road from Tianjin Dagu to Beijing!) This is not worth emulating. Now that Sai Jinhua is dead, has the era of Sai Jinhua also died with Sai Jinhua's death? This is worth savoring.

Wool Sweaters 196

— Fan Jia

The children in the alley have all put on wool sweaters, looking quite dashing sitting on their little tricycles. My four-year-old son secretly said to his mother that he wanted a wool sweater too. At the time, I didn't know what my wife said to answer her little darling.

Children always like to play in the alley. If one child in the group has a new toy or wears a new piece of clothing, the others will also want the same toy and clothing. This may be a characteristic of the alley I live in. There was a time when every child in this alley had an aviator cap. A friend came to see me and said that this alley had the air of an aviation school. This also shows that children like to be part of a group.

I don't know when it started, but tricycles became popular in the alley again. This toy is not as good as other things. For example, playing with a rubber ball or kicking shuttlecock is just dividing into two teams and competing to win or lose. Now it is a competition of who can ride their tricycle the fastest. As a result, quarrels often occur in the alley. Everyone has a desire to win, but playing with a rubber ball or kicking shuttlecock only results in the losing team wanting to play again, and the winning team shouting slogans happily. In the end, everyone enjoys themselves. But racing tricycles can lead to trouble. Riding fast can indeed take the lead, but if you can't control the handlebars, there is still a risk of hitting the wall. Moreover, if one tricycle derails, it will block another one. Therefore, when they can't make friends anymore, everyone abandons their tricycles and starts fighting.

After my child bought an aviator cap, he naturally wanted a tricycle as well, but I didn't allow him to. My reason for refusing him was that this thing would cause trouble. Maybe I'll buy him a foreign doll to play with in the future. The child is a good child. He doesn't understand the lies of adults. He is just dreaming a dream, a dream of a foreign doll.

Of course, the foreign doll has not been bought yet. Every day he sees me go out, he quietly asks me: "Dad, are you going to buy a foreign doll today?" I know he doesn't bluntly question me: "Dad, why haven't you bought a foreign doll yet!" because he's afraid I'll hit him. Seeing his pitiful appearance like that, a father is not a heartless snake after all. I nod and promise him that I will definitely buy one tonight. But when I get home, I only bring a few candies or a bag of candied chestnuts to coax him to have another good dream.

This time he wants a wool sweater, but he doesn't ask me. He asks his mother. The child is also a smart child. He has already seen through that his father is not a good person. If he thinks tricycles will cause trouble, does he also fear that foreign dolls will plot to kill for money? However, besides being able to hug him and tell him a story, his mother is just as good at lying as his father, and her lying skills are even better than his father's.

When I went out, the child was in the alley again. He stood at the foot of the wall on the sunny side, enviously watching his companions racing tricycles wearing wool sweaters. He didn't have either. The heroic appearance of the other children further accentuated his resemblance to a defeated rooster quietly kicked out of the circle by them. Seeing me come out, he ran over and grabbed my clothes, walking with me for a while. Only at the entrance of the alley did he ask me to buy a bag of candied chestnuts when I come back.

I coaxed him to go home, saying that his father would buy good things when he returned. With this wish in mind, I walked past many department stores, all of which were having big winter sales, but I couldn't find a wool sweater that I wanted to buy in my heart. On the way home, I bought an extra pear at the fruit store next to the candied chestnuts stand.

The child happily accepted these two good things. While eating, leaning against his mother's chest, he said to himself: "Dad will buy a wool sweater tomorrow."

I glanced at him, and my wife also glanced at him.

That night I read a few pages of a book, and suddenly remembered that there was still an old wool sweater of mine at the bottom of the chest. Taking it apart and knitting a sweater for the child would be more than enough. I told my wife, and she agreed, but she said that I should buy a new one for myself.

The next day, the wool was taken apart and washed. After being stretched on bamboo poles and dried in the sun, the child jumped around, touching it with his dirty hands, because his wife told him that the wool would be ready to knit a wool sweater for him after it was dry.

In a couple of days, the wool sweater was on the child's body. I opened the window, wanting to see his joy as he rejoined that group of children. Children should be allowed to move and live in their own world. But he was standing at the foot of the wall on the sunny side, still lacking a tricycle!

When my wife also leaned over, I closed the window.

People in Cages 197

— San San

—Prisoners of Guizhou

In the morning, when the shy sun sparingly casts its rays through the iron windows, many eyes will open, peering through the gaps in the "cage bars" and the iron window frames, affectionately looking at that small patch of daylight.

This is the beginning of another day.

As usual, the prison guard's assistant (we call him "the key holder") will come at this time to open the door and send a "watchman" out to call for water. During this period, the "gentlemen" in the "middle cage" have the opportunity to take a walk on the outside lawn.

Because they (the gentlemen) have money—giving several tens of dollars to the prison guard, several dollars to "the key holder," and another one or two dollars to several "watchmen"—they can reside in the "middle cage."

The "middle cage" is different from the "inner cage" in several ways. First, this place is relatively spacious and closer to the window. Second, only in the middle cage can one sleep on a high bed. Third, the prison guards treat them differently, allowing them to bring relatives and friends into the cage to talk with them. And fourth, they have longer "exercise" time.

What about the people in the "inner cage"? They are packed seven or eight to a cage. This cage is only about two square yards in size, surrounded on all sides by wooden bars as thick as small bowls (we call them "cage bars"). Only a few threads of sky can be vaguely seen through the gaps in the bars. Even on sunny days, it is still "dark and dismal" inside. Added to this are those dark, thin faces, making it seem little different from hell. The ground is dirt, always damp, and the people only use a straw mat or a few stalks of rice straw to sleep on. In the corner of the cage, a filthy bucket, even taller and bigger than a water bucket, emitting a foul odor, always accompanies them.

In hot weather, strings of bedbugs, crawling incessantly from the "cage bar" gaps, climb onto people's bodies, onto vegetables, and into the food. Moreover, they are not "nocturnal." No matter what time it is, if you don't spend a large amount of time fighting them, you won't get temporary peace. For one person, catching a hundred bedbugs every day

Page 19

is an easy task.

In cold weather, lice replace the bedbugs, attacking them.

The people in the cages, except for the very poor, provide for their own meals, either sent from home or by entrusting the watchmen to buy rice and vegetables and cook for themselves.

The penniless ones receive two or three cylinders of red unpolished rice (about two small bowls) from the prison every day, which doesn't expand much when cooked. Cooking dry rice can only yield three or four bowls, which of course cannot satisfy their needs for two meals. But they have no choice but to use some of it to exchange for water, coal, and vegetables. The remaining rice is only used for cooking porridge, with no other option. Year after year, they prolong their lives in thin porridge.

Every newcomer is locked in the inner cage. If his background is better, the prison guard will treat him as a "fat pig." If this "fat pig" doesn't know his place, beatings and shackles will be added to him, and he will even be forbidden from having his family send him food until he takes out money. Those who can only come up with five yuan will remain in the inner cage, and all they get is a cessation of abuse. Those who can come up with ten yuan or more can move to the middle cage.

Every new prisoner also has to be controlled by the "cage head" (the most senior and powerful person). You also have to give him some money, otherwise, he will torment you, make you sleep next to the toilet, and make you responsible for emptying the bucket every day.

The prison guards and "key holders" can beat and scold prisoners, needless to say. Even those watchmen who guard the prisoners in the cages (they live in the middle cage), if you don't give them some benefits, they will also reprimand you and prevent you from going outside to buy things.

Every day, from two o'clock to four o'clock, is the time for the prisoners to see the daylight. The key holder will release them into the outside open space.

Although this "exercise" time is stipulated by the yamen (government office), if the key holder is in a bad mood, it's useless, even if he doesn't let them exercise for several days. He doesn't care if the dung bucket overflows.

In the darkness, on the damp ground, in the foul air, and under the attack of bedbugs and lice, the underfed people are constantly getting sick and weakening, weakening... until the day they pray for (the day of their release) arrives, they are like birds locked up for a long time, finding it difficult to spread their wings.

Cao Xiaoying "Jade Dragonfly"

Sino-Western (1040) 1:00 PM to 1:45 PM

Opening "Palace Complaint"

The Western Palace is quiet at night, and hundreds of flowers are fragrant. Wanting to roll up the beaded curtain, one can't fight the endless hate. The imperial concubine sits alone on the agarwood couch. Burning red candles to await the king. Gao Lishi. Go tell the imperial concubine. Tonight, His Majesty is lodging in Zhaoyang Palace. Taizhen felt gloomy when she heard this. Wearily removing her makeup. Laying down on the mandarin duck quilt with her clothes on. Seeing a round bright moon shining on the palace wall. Sleeping lonely on a cold pillow, feeling sad and shedding tears. I advise people not to accompany the king. Accompanying the king is like accompanying a tiger. Thinking of the empress, what a beautiful face. Why was I abandoned on the sidelines? It's better to marry a romantic son. Enjoying pleasure morning and night. The crape myrtle flower facing the crape myrtle lover.

Master Yihong is an affectionate person. Thinking of the melancholic and sickly person. Putting on his bamboo hat and raincoat. Holding a lamp, he hurriedly walks to the garden. Walking to Xiaoxiang Hall. The girl just finished writing a poem and put down her pen. The maid suddenly reports that the Second Master has arrived. Only to see that his attire today is different from before. Brother Dou, why are you imitating a fisherman? The young master hears this and asks with concern. Is my sister's body at peace? Taking medicine and eating more, she should not write poetry recently. I am always worried. Therefore, I braved the rain to inquire clearly. If my sister likes this attire. I will send you a set on a good day. Pinqing replied, why is this needed? The image of a fisherwoman is truly worthless. Speaking these words, she secretly pondered, and should not have mentioned fisherman and fisherwoman. Peach blossom face flushes with shame, hard to hide. Silently bowing her head, she says nothing. One is unintentionally saying the wrong thing. One is not knowing love until its budding. The dream of the Red Chamber is full of changes. Briefly showing that, the paragraph where Xiaoxiang asks about sickness. Resenting the old man of the moon for not tying the threads of love. Therefore, medicine has no effect. In vain, two hearts.
