Echoes

The Great Shanghai Harmonica Company, in order to meet the needs of harmonica enthusiasts, has ordered a large number of type harmonicas from famous factories that have never been seen in Shanghai. They are fully stocked with A major, B major, G major, F major, etc. In addition, the harmonica class affiliated with the company does not charge any membership fees or tuition fees, so those who sign up to join are very enthusiastic. There are already more than 80 male and female members, and the class officially started yesterday. Harmonica expert Mr. Chen Jianchen was specially invited to teach. There are still some vacancies. Those interested in studying can go to participate today. Register soon or lose out. The address is No. 252, West Douwen Temple.

The Chinese Opera Troupe will print a selection of songs called "New Life of Love," using 200-pound wood pulp paper and exquisite printing. The reservation paper must be attached with 2 cents postage and sent to the Xinxin Radio Station on Nanjing Road or the Sino-Western Radio Station on Fourth Horse Road. Each person will receive two copies when it is published.

Movies

"With One Heart and Soul" in Nanjing 201

"With One Heart and Soul" began its test screening at the Xindu Theater in Nanjing on the 3rd, and the audience was very enthusiastic. On the evening of the test screening, many Nanjing reporters, writers, filmmakers, and socialites attended. Tian Han also accompanied his wife and beloved daughter Mary to visit. The playwright Hua Han was busy entertaining, attracting much attention from the audience.

The Nanjing newspapers competed to publish special issues. Xinmin Bao, Nanjing Daily, Ren Bao, Hua Bao, and Rotary Daily all mobilized their supplements to write articles recommending it. The Nanjing Daily even prepared a "Daily Movie" supplement and is currently planning a "With One Heart and Soul" reader symposium to specifically discuss the plot and performance of the film.

Mr. Tian Han wrote a large article in the Xinmin Bao introducing the film, saying: "At a time when various imperialists are vigorously preparing for the Second World War, when the Spanish warlords are colluding with fascist countries to drive Moorish troops and Kazakh troops to slaughter innocent people in the country, when the Chinese warlords, under the command of the 'friendly' military headquarters, are conducting a shameless war on the edge of Daqingshan, seeing the film 'With One Heart and Soul,' which is based on the heroic and moving story of the Chinese people enduring hardships and organizing the anti-imperialist and anti-warlord struggle, is very inspiring..."

"Ancient Tomb Adventure" 202

Showing at the Great Shanghai

Chen Qixia and Female Students 203

"Female Students" is a brilliant work co-directed by Shao Zuiweng and Wen Yimin after "On the Banks of the Huangpu River." It is also the second film starring the newcomer Chen Qixia. Since the public release of "On the Banks of the Huangpu River," everyone has generally recognized that Chen Qixia has a talent for acting, and in "Female Students," she has made even more rapid progress.

The male lead in "Female Students" is Tao Jin. He is the mainstay of the China Travel Theater. He first co-starred with Chen Qixia in "On the Banks of the Huangpu River," and already had very good results. This second collaboration will naturally not disappoint us either.

In "On the Banks of the Huangpu River," Chen Qixia played a commoner girl, while in "Female Students," she plays an aristocratic girl. She can play these two different types of personalities just right.

We can believe that after the public release of "Female Students," Chen Qixia's position on the screen will not only increase but also be established.

The Great Evening News Children's Friendship Association Performs "Ancient Temple Bells" 204

The Children's Friendship Association, launched by the Great Evening News, has been preparing for several months. It is now reported that the founding meeting is scheduled for 9:30 AM on the 13th of this month at the Carlton Theater on Park Road. In addition to singing and dancing performances and the children's song singing by the Shamei Children's Choir, there is also the Children's Friendship Association drama group's "Ancient Temple Bells." The playwright and director of this drama is Mr. Xu Xingzhi. It has been rehearsing for a month since the beginning, so it is predicted that the results will be satisfactory. According to the large-scale public performance of children's drama, it is still the first time in the history of the Chinese drama movement, and all parties are paying close attention to this drama.
